id='poem_sentence_2_544321_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='3cf9a89ad58144efbee6de8506eb2fde_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>，55岁</div><div id='3cf9a89ad58144efbee6de8506eb2fde' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>任提举常平，归休无锡，秋日游历张公洞，拜访杨万里，请其为《益斋藏书目》作序。作品：《游张公洞》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·史能之《咸淳毗陵志》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_58604' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58604' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58604?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张公洞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_58604")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_58604_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58604'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58604'>吾闻荆溪南，有地仙所宅。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58604'>十年劳梦想，今日著脚历。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58604'>扁舟下湖㳇，水涨没砂碛。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58604'>结缆小桥傍，杖藜从所适。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58604'>平冈面坡陁，叠嶂堆襞积。<div id='poem_sentence_4_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_58604'>行行三两里，夹道乔木植。<div id='poem_sentence_5_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_58604'>其末几合抱，其高乃千尺。<div id='poem_sentence_6_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_58604'>风生万壑响，日照四山赤。<div id='poem_sentence_7_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_58604'>时摇树林杪，忽见屋宇脊。<div id='poem_sentence_8_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_58604'>宫门何峥嵘，南路颇脩直。<div id='poem_sentence_9_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_58604'>长廊景曀曀，崩殿人寂寂。<div id='poem_sentence_10_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_58604'>寥落昔贤题，摩挲壁间墨。<div id='poem_sentence_11_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_58604'>扪萝上层岭，俯瞰得深窟。<div id='poem_sentence_12_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_58604'>危梯交枝撑，鸟道穿诘屈。<div id='poem_sentence_13_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_58604'>投身乍宽纵，跼步仍逼窄。<div id='poem_sentence_14_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_58604'>攀援愁颠跻，傲睨惊险僻。<div id='poem_sentence_15_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_58604'>悬崖朵颏颔，乱石拱剑戟。<div id='poem_sentence_16_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_58604'>白云何时横，乳溢或自滴。<div id='poem_sentence_17_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_58604'>中空正澒洞，了不见天隙。<div id='poem_sentence_18_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_58604'>冥行迷近远，伛偻犹擿埴。<div id='poem_sentence_19_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_58604'>巉岩岂人工，隐轸入地脉。<div id='poem_sentence_20_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_58604'>穷幽或篝火，俯跪仅容席。<div id='poem_sentence_21_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_58604'>仙坛尚故处，丹灶俨遗迹。<div id='poem_sentence_22_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_58604'>山虫鸣咿嚘，野鼠声啧唶。<div id='poem_sentence_23_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_58604'>传闻老父语，以往深莫测。<div id='poem_sentence_24_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_58604'>中有白玉堂，横绝巨石塞。<div id='poem_sentence_25_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_58604'>傍连洞庭野，欲去不可极。<div id='poem_sentence_26_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_58604'>潜窥目先旋，纵走膝无力。<div id='poem_sentence_27_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_58604'>邅回步西径，突兀出峭壁。<div id='poem_sentence_28_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_58604'>枞风高枝樛，藤蔓青阴羃。<div id='poem_sentence_29_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_58604'>芳草何芊绵，丹花亦狼籍。<div id='poem_sentence_30_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_58604'>踌躇古亭上，頫仰幽涧碧。<div id='poem_sentence_31_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_58604'>丁当下流水，磊磈欲落石。<div id='poem_sentence_32_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_58604'>虽云培塿高，气与嵩华敌。<div id='poem_sentence_33_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_58604'>其南有空穴，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_58604", 58604, "Clauses/69/Comments/0")'>澹瀩</span>殷幽黑。<div id='poem_sentence_34_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_58604'>阴风互吞吐，冷气森喷逼。<div id='poem_sentence_35_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_58604'>蛟龙久伏藏，金玉閟简册。<div id='poem_sentence_36_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_58604'>灵踪信茫昧，幻怪纷惨戚。<div id='poem_sentence_37_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_58604'>将无神物守，欲与世壤隔。<div id='poem_sentence_38_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_58604'>平生丘壑念，蚤岁泉石癖。<div id='poem_sentence_39_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_58604'>岂不思三山，所恨无六翮。<div id='poem_sentence_40_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_58604'>乐哉兹辰游，逸兴潜有激。<div id='poem_sentence_41_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_58604'>仙翁在何许，绿发尚如昔。<div id='poem_sentence_42_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_58604'>髣髴笙箫声，徘徊鸾鹤翼。<div id='poem_sentence_43_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_58604'>俗缘磨不尽，梦境坐形役。<div id='poem_sentence_44_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_58604'>何阶筑衡茅，幽讨穷日夕。<div id='poem_sentence_45_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_58604'>风云西北起，天地忽改色。<div id='poem_sentence_46_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_58604'>仓皇促归旆，造物岂戏剧。<div id='poem_sentence_47_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_58604'>良游易乖悟<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑当作牾）</span>，真赏难再得。<div id='poem_sentence_48_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_58604'>寄语山中人，重来傥相识<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_49_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_58604'></div><div id='poem_sentence_50_58604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_58604'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_49_58604_0'>⑴ 以上宋史能之《咸淳毗陵志》卷二三</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_58604_comment'></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>任提举常平，归休无锡之际应邀作文。作品：《雪巢记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·林表民《赤城集》卷一五。杨万里有《雪巢赋》）</span>《〈雪巢小集〉序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·林表民《赤城集》卷一七。杨万里亦有《〈雪巢小集〉序》）</span><div id='poem_1258662' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258662' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258662?labeling=true' target='_blank'>雪巢记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258662")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258662_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258662'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258662'>吴兴林君景思寓居天台城西之萧寺，破屋数椽，不庇风雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258662_comment'></div>榜其燕坐之室曰「雪巢」，日哦诗于其閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258662_comment'></div>客有问君所以名巢之意，君曰：「天下四时之佳景，宜莫如雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258662_comment'></div>而幻化变灭之速，亦无甚于雪者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258662_comment'></div>方其凝寒立水，夜气赑屃，纷纷皓皓，万里一色，瑶台银阙，亦见于俄顷閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258662_comment'></div>然朝阳熹晖，则向之所睹，荡然没灭而不留矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258662_comment'></div>自吾来居天台，时王公贵人比里而相望，朱门甲第击钟而鼎食，童颜稚齿群聚而嬉戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258662_comment'></div>今未二十年，其昔之贵者则已死，向之富者或已贫，而往之少者悉已耄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1258662_comment'></div>回视二十年，直俄顷尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1258662_comment'></div>其幻化变灭之速，不犹愈于雪乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1258662_comment'></div>知其非坚实也，于其俄顷起灭之中，乃复颠冥于利害，交战于宠辱，汩汩至于老死而不自知，非惑欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1258662_comment'></div>今吾以是名吾巢，且将视其虚以存吾心，视其白以见吾性，视其清以励吾节，视其幻以观吾生，则知少壮之不足恃，富贵之不足慕，贫与贱者不足以为戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1258662_comment'></div>非特以此自警，而且以警夫世之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1258662_comment'></div>使凡游吾之巢者，躁者可使静，险者可使平，而污者可使之洁，不亦休乎」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1258662_comment'></div>余闻而叹曰：浩哉斯巢，虽方丈之地，其视广厦万閒而不与易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1258662_comment'></div>夫乐莫乐于富贵，忧莫忧于贫贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1258662_comment'></div>然有马千驷，不如西山之饿夫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1258662_comment'></div>纡朱怀金，不如陋巷之瓢饮！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1258662_comment'></div>孰知乎匹夫之乐，有贤于王公大人之忧畏也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1258662_comment'></div>世之附炎之徒，方思炙手权门，焦头烂额而不悔，求而不得则躁，得而患失则戚，戚与躁相乘，则心火内焚，日夜焦灼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1258662_comment'></div>闻君之风，亦可少愧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1258662_comment'></div>君少尝从高僧问祖师西来意，又于方士得养生术，其清玉洁，其真行烈，其穷不堪忍，而其乐侃侃然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1258662_comment'></div>余来天台，始识君，一见如平生欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1258662_comment'></div>时方困郡事，卒卒无须臾閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1258662_comment'></div>每从君语，辄爽然自失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1258662_comment'></div>顾视鞭扑满前，牒诉盈几，便欲舍去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1258662_comment'></div>今得归休林泉之下，每一思君，发于梦想，则雪巢之境，恍然在吾目围中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1258662_comment'></div>因述君之说，使书于其壁，以为之记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1258662_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1258649' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258649' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258649?labeling=true' target='_blank'>雪巢小集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258649")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258649_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258649'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258649'>余友林宪景思，吴兴人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258649_comment'></div>年少时卓荦有大志，贺参政子忱奇其才，以孙女妻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258649_comment'></div>临终，复与米数百斛，谢不取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258649_comment'></div>贺既亡，挈其孥居萧寺，屡濒于馁而不悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258649_comment'></div>读书著文，不改其乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258649_comment'></div>顷尝随贺使虏，同行中后有鼎贵者，会赴大比试，来都城，因游西湖上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258649_comment'></div>新贵人于马上觇识之，使人传言请见，亟遁去，其操守如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258649_comment'></div>独喜哦诗，初不锻炼，而落笔立就，浑然天成，无一语蹈袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1258649_comment'></div>如「柔橹晚潮上，寒镫深树中」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1258649_comment'></div>「汲水延晚花，推窗数新竹」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1258649_comment'></div>「中夜鹅鹜喧，谁家海船上」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1258649_comment'></div>唐人之精于诗者不是过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1258649_comment'></div>一时名流皆愿交之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1258649_comment'></div>若徐敦立、芮国器、莫子及、毛平仲，相与为莫逆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1258649_comment'></div>其后诸公彫丧略尽，君亦连蹇不偶，至无屋可居，无田可耕，其贫益甚，其节益固，而其诗益工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1258649_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1258649_comment'></div>士患无才，而有才者，困穷类若此，岂发造化之秘，天殆恶此耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1258649_comment'></div>抑尝谓富与贵人之所可得，而才者天之所甚靳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1258649_comment'></div>景思取天之所甚靳者多，则不能兼人之所可得固宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1258649_comment'></div>然则才者实致穷之具，人何用有此，而天亦何用靳此，此未易以理晓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1258649_comment'></div>君所居室名曰雪巢，尝属余记之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1258649_comment'></div>故其诗若干篇，自号《雪巢小集》云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1258649_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='17244e756eb740d89a61706d8db7a30a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("17244e756eb740d89a61706d8db7a30a");'><span id='17244e756eb740d89a61706d8db7a30a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1190')">1189-1190年</a>，66-67岁</div><div id='17244e756eb740d89a61706d8db7a30a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年6月</a>　居无锡束带河大第;会晤周必大，书告杨万里。作品：《与杨廷秀书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·杨万里《诚斋集》卷六六《与周子充少保书》原作已佚。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>　在无锡，秋，受杨万里中洲茶，有诗寄之。作品：《杨廷秀寄中洲茶》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·杨万里《诚斋集》卷二五。原作已佚。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>　在无锡，秋，觅杨万里《道院集》，有诗寄之。作品：《觅杨廷秀〈道院集〉》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·杨万里《诚斋集》卷二五。原作已佚。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>　在无锡，秋，姜夔来访，与之论诗体。作品：《与姜尧章论诗体》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·姜夔《白石道人诗集》卷首《原序》）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年11月</a>　十一月，在家乡无锡家居。杨万里接伴北使，过苏州、无锡，有诗寄之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>　在无锡，乡居吟咏。作品：《玉簪花一名鹭鸶》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·方回《瀛奎律髓》卷二七。该篇所咏皆在玉簪花，抒发尤袤之孤直及不同时好而遭贬斥之境遇，当作于是年奉祠归里时。）</span><div id='poem_58562' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58562' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58562?labeling=true' target='_blank'>玉簪花一名鹭鸶</a><span class='authorDate'>（1189年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_58562")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58562_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58562'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58562'>一种幽花迥出尘，孤高耻逐艳阳辰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58562'>瑶枝巧插青鸾扇，玉蕊斜攲白鹭巾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58562'>难与松筠争岁晚，也同葵藿趁时新。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58562'>西风昨夜惊庭绿，满院清香恼杀人<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上同上书卷二七）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58562'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58562_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1190')">1190年1月</a>　正月，在家乡无锡家居，杨万里有诗寄赠。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1190')">1190年</a>　在无锡，乡居吟咏。作品：《落梅》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·方回《瀛奎律髓》卷二○。一作《瑞鹧鸪·咏落梅》词;考其“春事”的描绘，当作于是年初。）</span>《海棠盛开》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·方回《瀛奎律髓》卷二七。一作《瑞鹧鸪·海棠》词;考其“春事”的描绘，当作于是年初。）</span><div id='poem_58614' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58614' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58614?labeling=true' target='_blank'>瑞鹧鸪 落梅</a><span class='authorDate'>（1190年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_58614")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_58614_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58614'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58614'>清溪西<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作南）</span>畔小桥东，落月纷纷水映红<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58614'>五夜客愁花片里，一年春事角声中。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58614_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58614'>歌残玉树人何在，舞破山香曲未终。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58614'>却忆孤山醉归路，马蹄香<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作残）</span>雪衬东风。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58614'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_58614'><span class='label'>原注：</span>第二句未有别本可考。遂初诗，其孙新安半刺藻尝刊行，而焚于兵。予得其家所抄副本，颇有讹缺云。<br /><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_58614_0'>⑴ 《万柳溪边旧话》作落叶纷纷水映空</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_58614_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_58581' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58581' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58581?labeling=true' target='_blank'>海棠盛开<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup> 海棠</a><span class='authorDate'>（1190年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_58581")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58581_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_58581_0'>① 《万柳溪边旧话》引此诗亦作《瑞鹧鸪》词</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58581'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58581'>两株芳蕊傍池<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作溪）</span>阴，一笑嫣然抵万金。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58581'>火齐照林光灼灼，彤霞射水影沉沉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58581'>晓妆无力燕支重，春醉方酣酒晕深。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58581'>定自格高难著句，不应工部总无心<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58581'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_58581'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_58581_0'>⑴ 原注：酒晕一作酒醴，出《前汉书·董贤传》，注谓酒在醴中。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_58581_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>，70岁</div><div id='b967bf8f7223432397ce891688f1b090' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　归葬无锡西孔山。<br /></div>

class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258627' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258627?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐生日酒物表<span class='inlineComment2'>（代梁叔子）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年5月</a>　在京，五月，虞允文荐为秘书丞;始为杨万里所知。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年10月</a>　十月，在京，除知吉州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年10月24日</a>　十月二十四日，赴任吉州，途中跋次子尤槩于舟中钞录补足之南唐徐锴《说文系传》作品：《〈说文系传〉跋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（南唐·徐锴《说文系传》卷末。）</span><div id='poem_1258641' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258641' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258641?labeling=true' target='_blank'>说文系传跋</a><span class='authorDate'>（乾道九年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258641")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258641_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258641'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258641'>余暇日整比三馆乱书，得南唐徐楚金《说文系传》，爱其博洽有根据，而一半断烂不可读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258641_comment'></div>会江西漕刘文潜以书来，言李仁甫托访此书，乃从叶石林氏借得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258641_comment'></div>方传录未竟，而余有补外之命，遂令小子暨于舟中补足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258641_comment'></div>此本得于苏魏公家，而讹舛尚多，当是未经校理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258641_comment'></div>乾道癸巳十月廿四日，尤袤题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1258641_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年11月</a>　未到吉州任，即中途折返。十一月，回京，因太子庶子、谕德阙官，专差讲《礼记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年7月</a>　以梁克家荐，召对，除吏部员外郎;七月初，与周必大书函往来，问其病情。作品：《与周子充知院必大札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·周必大《文忠集》卷一八九《与尤延之侍郎袤札子》原作已佚;周必大有复信《与尤延之侍郎袤札子》（淳熙十年））</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年7月</a>　七月，在京奏论荒政。作品：《论救荒之政奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·马端临《文献通考》卷二六。）</span><div id='poem_1258613' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258613' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258613?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论救荒之政奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙十年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258613")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258613_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258613'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258613'>东南民力凋弊，中人之家，至无数月之储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258613_comment'></div>前年旱伤，江东之南康，江西之兴国，俱是小垒，南康饥民一十二万二千有奇，兴国饥民七万二千有奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258613_comment'></div>且祖宗盛时，荒政著闻者，莫如富弼之在青州，赵抃之在会稽，在当时已是非常之灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258613_comment'></div>夷考其实，则青州一路饥民止十五万，几及南康一军之数；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258613_comment'></div>会稽大郡，饥民才二万二千而已，以兴国较之，已是三倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258613_comment'></div>至于振赡之米，弼用十五万，抃用三万六千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258613_comment'></div>今江东公私合力振救，为米一百四十二万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258613_comment'></div>去岁江西振济兴国一军，除民间劝诱所得，出于官者，自当七万，其视青州一路，会稽一郡，所费实相倍蓰，则知今日公私诚是困竭，不宜复有小歉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1258613_comment'></div>国家水旱之备，止有常平、义仓，频年旱暵，发之略尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1258613_comment'></div>今所以为预备之计，唯有多出缗钱，广储米斛而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1258613_comment'></div>愿预饬有司随市价禁科抑，则人自乐输，必易集事。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1258613_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年10月3日</a>　十月三日，以吏部员外郎兼太子侍讲。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年6月11日</a>　六月十一日铨试，任考官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年8月</a>　八月，除枢密院检详文字兼太子侍讲。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年9月15日</a>　九月十五日，在京应邀作文。作品：《刑部郎官题名记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·潜说友《咸淳临安志》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_1258660' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258660' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258660?labeling=true' target='_blank'>刑部郎官题名记</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙十一年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258660")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258660_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258660'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258660'>合天下讼狱之成，律令章程之事，悉总于尚书刑部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258660_comment'></div>其轻重出入之际，人之死生系焉，责任为不轻矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258660_comment'></div>唐制刑部郎分四司，曰刑部，曰都官，曰比部，曰司门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258660_comment'></div>本朝因之，然止以为阶官，不釐本务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258660_comment'></div>凡四方以具狱来上，则谳于审刑院，别命朝官一员判院事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258660_comment'></div>至于元丰，始以审刑归刑部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258660_comment'></div>官制行，二十四司各正其职，于是刑部始得专其官，而任益重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258660_comment'></div>中兴以来，遵承不改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1258660_comment'></div>圣天子哀矜庶狱，郎官必采时望，非明习法令更治民者弗除，所以选任之意甚厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1258660_comment'></div>士之当是选者，可不思所以称明指哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1258660_comment'></div>夫法者，一成而不可变者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1258660_comment'></div>民伪日滋，法不能胜，奇请它比，纷然杂陈于前，居其任者，苟非明有以察之，仁有以守之，公有以行之，则奸吏并缘，舞文巧诋，人受其害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1258660_comment'></div>故居官称职，每难其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1258660_comment'></div>而在上者，尤以择贤任职为意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1258660_comment'></div>岁月既久，除授不一，前人名氏，漫不可考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1258660_comment'></div>淳熙十一年，陈公倚、钱公冲之之为是官也，慨然兴叹，谋欲序次而书之石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1258660_comment'></div>会钱公移漕畿甸，乃伐石庀工，祝陈公绪成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1258660_comment'></div>繇绍兴末得七十人，属袤记其事，且曰：「视其名而考其岁月，则其人之功行善最，皆可枚数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1258660_comment'></div>使后之居于斯者，有所警而不敢忽也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1258660_comment'></div>乃述其大略，且使知刑部之有题名，自二公始云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1258660_comment'></div>九月望。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1258660_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年</a>　在京因陆九渊之请，为其岳父作墓志铭。作品：《吴公墓志》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·李子愿《象山先生年谱》（雍正十年刻本）卷中。陆九渊于是年九月既望作《宋故吴公行状》，则该篇当作于此后不久，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_1258667' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258667' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258667?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吴公墓志</a><span class='authorDate'>（1184年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258667")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258667_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258667'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258667'>陆君子静数为予道其妇翁吴公之贤，居亡何，有墨服踵门而求见者，则吴公之子颙若也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258667_comment'></div>袖子静之状，且告曰：「敢因子静以请志」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258667_comment'></div>予不识吴公，然子静信人也，其言有證，乃叙而志之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258667_comment'></div>夫识子静于童稚之中，而能以子妻之，其贤可知矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1258667_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1258667'><span class='label'>按：</span>《象山先生年谱》卷中，雍正十年刻本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1258667_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年</a>　在京襄助朱熹安葬朱弁，并应熹托为弁作墓志铭。作品：《奉使直秘阁朱公墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·朱熹《晦庵先生朱文公文集》卷九八。原作已佚;据朱熹《奉使直秘阁朱公行状》所述，其时尤袤居官枢密院检详文字，故系于此。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年11月</a>　十一月，兼国史院编修官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年</a>　冬日，于紫宸殿有贺雪之作。作品：《入紫宸殿贺雪》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·杨万里《诚斋集》卷一九。原作已佚。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年</a>　在京参与张栻文集的编辑。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年12月3日</a>　十二月三日，在京与周必大论家藏苏舜钦《四时歌》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年</a>　林宪应举落第后，有诗寄之。作品：《寄林景思》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·林表民《天台续集别编》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_58582' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58582' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58582?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄林景思</a><span class='authorDate'>（1184年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_58582")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58582_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58582'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58582'>临海睽离七度春，都城相见话悲辛。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58582'>苍颜白发浑非旧，短句长篇却有神。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58582'>一第蹉跎真可叹，半生奔走坐长贫。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58582'>老怀先<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：去声。）</span>自难为别，相识如君更几人<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58582'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_58582'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_58582_0'>⑴ ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年2月</a>　二月，在京有诗寄杨万里。作品：《右司郎署疏竹》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·杨万里《诚斋集》卷一九。原作已佚。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年3月4日</a>　在京，三月四日，与朱熹书，并封送主管华州云台观敕命及朱弁墓志铭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年3月</a>　在京，三月，跋范仲淹与尹师鲁手启墨迹。作品：《范文正公与尹师鲁二帖》<span class='inlineComment2'>（明·赵琦美《赵氏铁网珊瑚》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1258640' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258640' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258640?labeling=true' target='_blank'>范文正公与尹师鲁二帖跋</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙十二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258640")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258640_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258640'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258640'>方范文正因与吕文靖争论上前贬饶州时，尹舍人实上书愿得俱贬，监郢州酒税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258640_comment'></div>此一卷帖，情义谆谆，不啻兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258640_comment'></div>盖二公爱君忧国，道合志同，其相与之厚，自应尔耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258640_comment'></div>淳熙乙巳清明日，梁溪尤袤敬观。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1258640_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a>　在京，进诗论郊祀大礼。作品：《郊祀大礼庆成诗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南宋馆阁续录》卷五。原作已佚。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a>　以右司郎官分领封椿库，辞。五月十九日，差何万兼领。作品：《辞领封椿库奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（清·徐松《宋会要辑稿》食货五一之一二。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年11月1日</a>　在京，十一月初一，书陈公亮《重建严先生祠堂记》<br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_0_58576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58576'>饱闻治最誇闽部，已有先声到益都。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58575'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58575_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年6月15日</a>　在京，六月十五日，题王厚之所藏《兰亭帖》作品：《题王顺伯第一本》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·桑世昌《兰亭考》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1258638' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258638' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258638?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题王顺伯第一本</a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年6月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258638")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258638_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258638'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258638'>定武《兰亭》旧本，在承平时已不易得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258638_comment'></div>薛师正之子绍彭刻他本易去，而于旧石斲损数字以惑人，后以石龛置宣和殿壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258638_comment'></div>渡江以来，士大夫家凡得此本，悉指为定武本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258638_comment'></div>不但肥瘦不同，而精彩顿异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258638_comment'></div>其「竹」字、「托」字，宛转处与「夫」字、「人」字末笔意态横生，非他本可及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258638_comment'></div>比斲去本自不多见，况未经薛氏所斲之本乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258638_comment'></div>此本旧所拓，尤可贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258638_comment'></div>余见《兰亭叙》多矣，此特一二见尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1258638_comment'></div>淳熙丙午季夏望日，尤袤延之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1258638_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>　在京，秋日，题周必大家藏苏轼《子高》、《无雪》二帖。作品：《题东坡〈子高〉、〈无雪〉二帖》<span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>　获赐孝宗手录《汉书》列传，以之示杨万里，杨有《跋尤延之左司所藏光尧御书歌》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年9月</a>　在京，九月，与杨万里、京镗论王淮为嫡子报服事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>　在京，作山水两轴，杨万里有《跋尤延之山水两轴》七绝二首。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年1月</a>　在京，立春后一日，和张镃诗，有“冰柱”句。作品：《立春后一日和张功父园梅未开韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·杨万里《诚斋集》卷二一。原作已佚;杨万里有《立春后一日，和张功父〈园梅未花〉之韵》）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年1月20日</a>　在京，正月二十日，差于别试所考试。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年3月3日</a>　三月初三，同杨万里、林宪等游西湖。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年3月</a>　在京，三月，封送主管南京鸿庆宫敕命与朱熹。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年4月6日</a>　四月六日，与洪迈等同观沈揆所藏《兰亭序》帖于秘书省之群玉亭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>　王信假礼部尚书使金，与同僚为之饯行，再观沈揆所藏《兰亭序》帖。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年5月</a>　五月，同杨万里、京镗等在西湖设酒为客人送行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年5月25日</a>　五月二十五日，升兼太子左谕德，申言民贫兵怨。作品：《论兵民奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·脱脱等《宋史》卷三八九《尤袤传》原作已佚。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年7月</a>　在京，七月，应诏上封事，论救荒之策。作品：《应诏上封事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·马端临《文献通考》卷二六。）</span><div id='poem_1258614' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258614' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258614?labeling=true' target='_blank'>应诏上封事</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙十年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258614")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258614_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258614'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258614'>天地之气，宣通则和，壅遏则乖；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258614_comment'></div>人心舒畅则悦，抑郁则愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258614_comment'></div>催科峻急而农民怨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258614_comment'></div>关征苛察而商旅怨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258614_comment'></div>差注留滞，而士大夫有失职之怨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258614_comment'></div>廪给脧削，而士卒有不足之怨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258614_comment'></div>奏谳不时报，而久系囚者怨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258614_comment'></div>幽枉不获伸，而负累者怨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1258614_comment'></div>强暴杀人，多特贷命，使已死者怨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1258614_comment'></div>有司买纳，不即酬价，负贩者怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1258614_comment'></div>人心抑郁所以感伤天和者，岂特一事而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1258614_comment'></div>方今救荒之策，莫急于劝分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1258614_comment'></div>昨者朝廷立赏格以募出粟，富家忻然输纳，故庚子之旱不费支吾者，用此策也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1258614_comment'></div>自后输纳既多，朝廷吝于推赏，多方沮抑，或恐富家以命令为不信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1258614_comment'></div>乞诏有司检举行之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1258614_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>　在京，秋，应邀与杨万里、京镗等人，秋日至张镃桂隐轩赏花，互有唱和。作品：《功父桂隐花开，蒙邀赏，和韵以谢之》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·张镃《南湖集》卷五。原作已佚。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年9月10日</a>　九月十日，同杨万里至临安南山观净慈新殿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年9月10日</a>　与杨万里、京镗等同游临安刘寺展绣亭、灵芝寺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>　在京，居西掖时，有诗寄黄宗谅。作品：《寄黄宗谅》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·楼钥《攻愧集》卷一〇四《黄仲友墓志铭》据楼钥“尤公袤时居西掖”的提法，其时尤袤居官中书省，则该篇当作于为检正时，据任此官职之下限，姑系于此。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>　在京，获赵蕃所寄《赠尤检正四首》诗篇，与杨万里、陆游并称。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年10月7日</a>　十月七日，因周必大荐，除太常少卿，兼太子左谕德。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>　在京，与王淮论五使事，以为攒宫不当置。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年10月17日</a>　高宗薨后，十月十七日，与颜师鲁、郑侨等共论庙号不当称“祖”。诏送集议所。作品：《大行太上皇帝庙号疏》2篇。<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·李心传《建炎杂记•甲集》卷二。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年10月21日</a>　在京，十月二十一日，论引见金国人使当在小祥两日后。作品：《论引见金国人使疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（清·徐松《宋会要辑稿》食货仪制八之二二。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年11月1日</a>　在京，十一月初一，与颜师鲁同上奏。作品：《乞大祥礼毕改服小祥之服奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·李心传《建炎杂记•乙集》卷三。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年12月18日</a>　在京，十二月十八日，与宇文价、颜师鲁、倪思、黄黼等同上疏。作品：《论贺正使不当却疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·李心传《建炎杂记•乙集》卷三。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>　在京，冬日，拜访张镃未果。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>　在京，与杨万里联名疏荐蔡元定于朝。作品：《荐蔡元定章》<span class='inlineComment2'>（明·蔡有鹍《蔡氏九儒书》卷二《西山公集》附录。据《宋史•蔡元定传》所述“太常少卿尤袤、秘书少监杨万里联疏荐于朝”，则该篇当作于是年冬或明年春，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_1258617' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258617' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258617?labeling=true' target='_blank'>荐蔡元定章</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙十五年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258617")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258617_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258617'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258617'>臣袤叨恩太常，无毫补报，惟有推贤，少尽万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258617_comment'></div>伏念教化乃刑政之本，人才实教化之原，不有奖劝，何以使人激励而兴起？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258617_comment'></div>臣常咨访，得其人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258617_comment'></div>切见建阳布衣蔡元定，资禀颖异，充养完粹，守分安贫，不求闻达，有经世济物之才，有制礼作乐之具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258617_comment'></div>早从朱熹学，熹尊为老友，则其才德必有大过人者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258617_comment'></div>隐贲西山，户屦常满，则其学识非人所能及者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258617_comment'></div>诚圣世之真儒，后学之师表也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258617_comment'></div>今元定身虽韬光于林壑，心实以治平为己任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1258617_comment'></div>陛下若起元定而用之，使与朱熹同侍经筵，必能光昭圣德，为国家立万世无疆之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1258617_comment'></div>其于治道，岂小补益而已哉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1258617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1258617'><span class='label'>按：</span>《西山公集》，蔡氏九儒书卷二。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1258617_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年1月9日</a>　在京任太常少卿兼太子左谕德，正月初九，献书于太子。作品：《献皇太子书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·李心传《建炎杂记•乙集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1258628' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258628' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258628?labeling=true' target='_blank'>献皇太子书</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙十五年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258628")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258628_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258628'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258628'>大权所在，天下之所争趋，甚可惧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258628_comment'></div>愿殿下事无大小，一取上旨而后行，情无厚薄，一付众议而后定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258628_comment'></div>且利害之端，常伏于思虑之所不到，疑閒之萌，每开于堤防之所不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258628_comment'></div>储副之位，止于侍膳问安，不交外事，抚军监国，自汉至今，多出权宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258628_comment'></div>事权不一，动有触碍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258628_comment'></div>乞候祔庙之后，便行恳辞，以彰殿下之令德。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1258628_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年1月16日</a>　正月十六日，密以札子禀东宫。作品：《禀东宫札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·周必大《文忠集》卷一七二《思陵录》上。原作已佚。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年3月</a>　在京，三月，乞禁释、老之教。作品：《论禁释老之教疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·脱脱等《宋史》卷三八九《尤袤传》）</span><br /></div><div class='label1' id='faaabba8e90f49d79d9a222ce4ee6659_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("faaabba8e90f49d79d9a222ce4ee6659");'><span id='faaabba8e90f49d79d9a222ce4ee6659_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1189')">1188-1189年</a>，65-66岁</div><div id='faaabba8e90f49d79d9a222ce4ee6659' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年4月</a>　在京，杨万里送《西归集》、《朝天集》，有诗论之。作品：《蒙杨廷秀送〈西归〉、〈朝天〉二集赠以七言》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·杨万里《诚斋集》卷二四附。据杨万里和诗自注“新归自朝陵所”，则尤袤该篇当作于是年四月的临安，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_58588' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58588' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58588?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蒙杨廷秀送西归朝天二集赠以七言</a><span class='authorDate'>（1188年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_58588")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58588_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58588'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58588'>西归累岁却朝天，添得囊中六百篇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58588'>垂棘连城三倍价，夜光明月十分圆。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58588'>竞誇凤沼诗仙样，当有鸡林贾客传。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58588'>我似岑参与高适，姓名得入少陵编<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋杨万里《诚斋集》卷二四附）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58588'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58588_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年</a>　在京，与杨万里论《易》之八卦，杨以《屯》等八卦求教。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年4月16日</a>　四月十六日，请诏群臣再集议配享臣僚。作品：《论缓定配飨疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·李心传《建炎杂记•乙集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1258618' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258618' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258618?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论缓定配飨疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙十五年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258618")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258618_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258618'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258618'>窃考祖宗典故，既祔庙然后议配飨，盖必先有庙而后有从祀之臣，礼则然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258618_comment'></div>赵普、曹彬之配食太庙，定议于二十馀年之后；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258618_comment'></div>薛居正、潘美配食太宗，议定于二年之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258618_comment'></div>乾兴元年，翰林学士李维等乞以王旦配食真宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258618_comment'></div>在祔庙后一月，最为切近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258618_comment'></div>然当时亦必诏礼官参议，务尽众言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258618_comment'></div>独嘉祐八年议以王曾、吕夷简配食仁宗，乃在山陵之前，然亦必先降诏旨，下两制定议当用何人，而王圭等始以曾等姓名上之，其不敢仓卒如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258618_comment'></div>元祐元年，裕陵复土已七阅月，有司始援典故，乞自两制以上及太常寺秘书省长贰同议配飨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1258618_comment'></div>又两月，而吏部尚书孙永等始以富弼应诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1258618_comment'></div>盖宗庙至重，必严其事，不病其缓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1258618_comment'></div>今来高宗犹未祔庙，所议配飨，少迟旬月，固未为晚，乃忽定于灵驾发引一日之先，事出仓卒，众以为疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1258618_comment'></div>仰惟高宗皇帝受命中兴，一时将相依乘风云，勒功帝籍，不出数人，自有公论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1258618_comment'></div>为之子孙，皆以祖考得预为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1258618_comment'></div>倘不按典故，不集众论，则无以厌服其他勋臣子孙之心，消弭众多之口，而祖宗集议典礼，将恐遂废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1258618_comment'></div>袤等备员礼官，诚见议论纷纷，以定配为速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1258618_comment'></div>以不集议为疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1258618_comment'></div>既有前件典故，倘不条陈，是为失职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1258618_comment'></div>欲乞候升祔礼毕，别择日下侍从、两省、台谏、礼官及秘书省集议施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1258618_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1258618'>〔小贴子〕：窃惟配食清庙，系大典礼，付之众人，则议论自公；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1258618_comment'></div>迟以岁月，则名实自定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1258618_comment'></div>公则人无异辞，定则万世不变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1258618_comment'></div>若韩琦之升配英庙，在当时孰有出其右者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1258618_comment'></div>然尤迟至九年之后，至熙宁末始降指挥，可见先朝不肯容易如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1258618_comment'></div>苟惟不然，王安石、蔡确之不合众心，虽定于绍圣、崇宁，而卒改正于绍兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1258618_comment'></div>今来亦宜反复熟议，以尽众言，少迟旬月，以待论定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1258618_comment'></div>庶几得预者无愧，不预者无辞。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1258618_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年4月</a>　在京，四月，与朱熹书函往来，论其辞请之事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年4月</a>　在京，四月，再议配享。作品：《乞俟丧毕再议升配奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·脱脱等《宋史》卷三八九《尤袤传》）</span><div id='poem_1258619' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258619' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258619?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞俟丧毕再议升配奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙十五年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258619")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258619_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258619'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258619'>方在几筵，不可配帝，且历举郊岁在丧服中者凡四，惟元祐明堂用吕大防请，升配神考，时去大祥止百馀日，且祖宗悉用以日易月之制，故升侑无嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258619_comment'></div>今陛下行三年之丧，高宗虽已祔庙，百官犹未吉服，讵可近违绍兴而远法元祐升侑之礼？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258619_comment'></div>请俟丧毕议之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1258619_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年4月26日</a>　四月二十六日，权礼部侍郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年5月11日</a>　在京，五月十一日，上疏乞裁定将来明堂大礼所设神位。作品：《乞裁定将来明堂大礼所设神位奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（清·徐松《宋会要辑稿》礼二四之九八。）</span><div id='poem_1258620' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258620' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258620?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞裁定将来明堂大礼所设神位奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙十五年五月十一日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258620")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258620_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258620'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258620'>伏睹已降御札，今岁九月有事于明堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258620_comment'></div>今照得逐次明堂大礼沿革：绍兴四年、七年、十年，设昊天上帝、皇地祇、太祖皇帝、太宗皇帝并天皇大帝已下从祀，共四百四十三位；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258620_comment'></div>绍兴三十一年明堂大礼，设昊天上帝、徽宗皇帝、五方帝、五人帝、五官神从祀，共一十七位；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258620_comment'></div>淳熙六年、九年明堂大礼，设昊天上帝、皇地祇、太祖皇帝、太宗皇帝并天皇大帝已下从祀，共七百七十一位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258620_comment'></div>今来缘高宗皇帝几筵未除，考于典礼，未合升配。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258620_comment'></div>所有将来明堂大礼所设神位，伏乞敷奏取旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1258620_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年5月14日</a>　在京，五月十四日，奏请皇帝于后殿视事。作品：《乞于后殿视事奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（清·徐松《宋会要辑稿》礼三五之一。）</span><div id='poem_1258621' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258621' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258621?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞于后殿视事奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙十五年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258621")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258621_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258621'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258621'>检准《国朝会要》，嘉祐八年三月二十九日，仁庙之丧，英宗七月十三日始御紫宸殿见群臣，退御垂拱殿，中书、枢密以次奏事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258621_comment'></div>盖始御内朝，犹未御正衙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258621_comment'></div>今外朝内朝皆未临御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258621_comment'></div>窃详后殿及延和殿乃祖宗崇政施化之所，缘今来延和地步窄隘，难以排立侍从、史官、管军、御带、环列、禁卫等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258621_comment'></div>今参酌欲乞皇帝于后殿视事，所有仪制，乞下閤门、禁卫所条具申尚书省。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1258621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1258621'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋会要辑稿》礼三五之一（第二册第一三○○页）。又见同书仪制五之三三（第二册第一九三二页）。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1258621_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年5月</a>　在京，五月，命与宋之瑞并监测淳熙日历。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年6月2日</a>　六月二日，以疾告，改命吏部侍郎章森与宋之瑞同往监测淳熙日历。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年6月</a>　在京，六月，上疏乞裒高宗御集及立阁名。作品：《乞裒高宗御集及立阁名奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·周必大《文忠集》卷一七三《思陵录》下。原作已佚。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年6月</a>　六月，以权礼部侍郎兼同修国史、实录院同修撰撰。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年</a>　在京，因忙于撰写《高宗皇帝实录》，请权罢国史院同修撰。<br /><a href="javascript: class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258623' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258623?labeling=true' target='_blank'>言攻道学之非疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1189年1月）</span><span id='poem_sentence_1_1258623_comment'></div>此名一立，贤人君子欲自见于世，一举足且入其中，俱无得免，此岂盛世所宜有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258623_comment'></div>愿徇名必责其实，听言必观其行，人才庶不坏于疑似。</div><div id='poem_title_1258630_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258630'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258630'>右袤启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258630_comment'></div>屈临都骑，宠贶华编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258630_comment'></div>集工部之诗，恍如己作；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258630_comment'></div>伏惟梦锡先辈，学追前辈，名动一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258630_comment'></div>独草玄文，喜家声之未泯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258630_comment'></div>屈居王后，知世德之方昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1258630_comment'></div>南山讵隐于豹章，北海即看于鹏运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1258630_comment'></div>不图暮景，获预荣观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1258630_comment'></div>流水高山，敢自期于真赏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1258630_comment'></div>夜光明月，应己悔于暗投。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1258630_comment'></div>颂咏之私，叙陈奚究。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1258630_comment'></div></div></div><br class='authorDate'>（1192年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年7月15日</a>　在京，七月十五日，跋曾敏行《独醒杂志》作品：《〈独醒杂志〉跋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·曾敏行《独醒杂志》（知不足斋刊本）附录。）</span><div id='poem_1258651' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258651' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258651?labeling=true' target='_blank'>独醒杂志跋<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍熙三年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1192年7月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258651")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258651_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258651'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258651'>浮云居士曾公以文学行义有声江西，予恨不识其人，而获从其子监簿游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258651_comment'></div>文献彬彬，所谓能世其家者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258651_comment'></div>一日，见公所著《独醒杂志》十卷，前言往行，登载不遗，有补于世，语简事核，非其他稗官小说之比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258651_comment'></div>读其书，想其人，如亲见其抵掌谈论，益知监簿家学渊源所从来远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258651_comment'></div>呜呼，士君子抱负所有，不见于用，必托于言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258651_comment'></div>若公者高见远识，尚友前辈，虽陆沈于下，而遗书满家，足以垂世传后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258651_comment'></div>其视富贵无闻者，孰得孰失？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258651_comment'></div>况又有子方骎骎显荣，足以为不亡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1258651_comment'></div>因书其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1258651_comment'></div>绍熙壬子孟秋望日，锡山尤袤题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1258651_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　任给事中日，屡有论驳。作品：《论驳除奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·脱脱等《宋史》卷三八九《尤袤传》原作已佚。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　韩侂胄以武功大夫、和州防御使用应办赏直转横行，缴奏之。作品：《缴韩侂冑转官》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·脱脱等《宋史》卷三八九《尤袤传》）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　韩侂冑转官奏入，手诏令书行，复奏，命遂格。作品：《再缴韩侂冑转官》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·脱脱等《宋史》卷三八九《尤袤传》）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年11月</a>　光宗以疾，一再不省重华宫，十一月，上封事。作品：《谏不省重华宫封事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·脱脱等《宋史》卷三八九《尤袤传》）</span><div id='poem_1258626' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258626' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258626?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谏不省重华宫封事<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍熙三年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1192年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258626")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258626_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258626'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258626'>寿皇事高宗历二十八年如一日，陛下所亲见，今不待倦勤以宗社付陛下，当思所以不负其托，望勿惮一日之勤，以解都人之惑。</div><div id='poem_sentence_0_1258626_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　林大中以论事左迁，率左史楼钥论奏。作品：《缴林大中辞免权吏部侍郎除直宝文阁事与郡》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·楼钥《攻愧集》卷二七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　耶律适嘿复以手诏除承宣使，一再缴奏。作品：《缴耶律适嘿除承宣使》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·脱脱等《宋史》卷三八九《尤袤传》）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　在京，力言中宫谒家庙推赏官吏一百七十二人之滥，乞痛裁节，光宗从之。作品：《乞裁节滥赏奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·脱脱等《宋史》卷三八九《尤袤传》原作已佚。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　在京，申言废法用例之弊。作品：《申论废法用例之弊奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·脱脱等《宋史》卷三八九《尤袤传》原作已佚。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　在京，出示家藏《葛仙翁徙居图》与楼钥，楼氏有题诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　在京，跋徐寿卿所藏《乐毅论》碑。作品：《跋徐仁叔藏〈乐毅论〉》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·陈槱《负暄野录》卷上。据陈槱《负暄野录》“尤延之给事袤”的提法，尤袤是跋当作于任给事中时，具体时间难以考证，姑系于此。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　知平江府沈揆修复虎丘古石井泉，并有诗论之；袤继范成大之后有次韵。作品：《石井泉次沈太守韵》3首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（清·顾湄《虎丘山志》卷二。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　在京，跋王明清所题《兰亭序帖》作品：《跋〈兰亭帖〉》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·桑世昌《兰亭考》卷七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年1月11日</a>　正月十一日，除礼部尚书，楼钥撰制词;仍兼实录院同修撰。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　在京，受王蔺之托，为其父王之道撰神道碑。作品：《赠故太师王公神道碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·王之道《相山集》卷三〇。王蔺于是年三月除知江陵府，则尤袤此篇当作于之前，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_1258668' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258668' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258668?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠故太师王公神道碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258668")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258668_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258668'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258668'>淳熙十有六年正月，寿皇圣帝将逊位，以今端明殿学士、通奉大夫、提举临安府洞霄宫王公蔺自礼部尚书为参知政事，诏有司宠其先世，于是赠皇考故朝奉大夫之道为太子少师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258668_comment'></div>阅月，上践阼，覃及天下，加赠太子太师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258668_comment'></div>四月，迁知枢密院事，赠少师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258668_comment'></div>明年，拜枢密使，加赠太师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258668_comment'></div>枢使罢政还故乡，周视松槚，乃谋刻其先德于墓之碑，而以其辞属袤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258668_comment'></div>于是太师之薨，盖二十有五年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258668_comment'></div>曩建炎间，敌侵江浙，长淮千里，莽为盗区，握兵者畏避不敢战，有城者遁逃不能守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258668_comment'></div>太师以一书生，率数千乌合之众，保胡避山以抗群贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1258668_comment'></div>区区一隅之地，东有张琪，南有邵青，西有李成，北有李伸，合其兵数千万，环布四境，磨牙有毒，卒不能吞噬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1258668_comment'></div>使一方之民仰事俯育，脱死锋刃，公之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1258668_comment'></div>不幸忤触权臣，才不究于用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1258668_comment'></div>而遗庆所钟，乃在其子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1258668_comment'></div>枢使既致位二府，为时名臣，而公赠官一品，荣耀身后，非阴德之报欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1258668_comment'></div>袤待罪史官，方裒次建炎以来故事，如公言议风烈，法所当载，故不敢辞，而为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1258668_comment'></div>按公字彦猷，无为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1258668_comment'></div>曾祖讳用和，隐德不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1258668_comment'></div>祖讳□，赠太保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1258668_comment'></div>考讳奇，累赠太傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1258668_comment'></div>曾祖妣冯氏、祖妣于氏，赠卫国夫人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1258668_comment'></div>妣施氏，累赠福国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1258668_comment'></div>公幼颖悟，八岁通一经，弱冠贡辟雍，与兄之义、弟之深同登宣和六年进士第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1258668_comment'></div>搢绅荣之，榜其所居堂曰三桂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1258668_comment'></div>时太平久，用事者开边隙，公知必乱，对策极言，考官恶其直，寘之下列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1258668_comment'></div>靖康初，调和州历阳丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1258668_comment'></div>县有大圩，积雨将败，皆豪家所占，请于官，欲增埂，郡檄公督役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1258668_comment'></div>公呼诸豪谕之曰：「尔圩尔修，将责之谁」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1258668_comment'></div>鞭其不率者，皆争出夫，得数千人，捍水而圩全，岁乃大熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1258668_comment'></div>郡以为能，俾摄令乌江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1258668_comment'></div>甫视事，御营使刘光世檄言大军且至，令具刍粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1258668_comment'></div>视仓库无铢粒，里豪素服恩信，不移晷得钱七十万，米三千斛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1258668_comment'></div>事定，悉以偿之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1258668_comment'></div>或谓军兴科借不必偿，公曰：「信不可去也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1258668_comment'></div>民相信，何忧匮乏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1258668_comment'></div>宣抚司檄清野，期以三日责军令状，公曰：「敌未至而先困吾民，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1258668_comment'></div>谴吾自当之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1258668_comment'></div>即书以授使者，令民安堵如故，不踰旬，清野之议亦寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1258668_comment'></div>以循资丐罢，奉二亲还乡，率族党保胡避山，使其弟之深守之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1258668_comment'></div>公以兵法部其丁壮，转战于外，且诱乡民运粟于山，能致一石者与其半，故粮不乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1258668_comment'></div>山西有毛公寨，李伸围之急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1258668_comment'></div>公以精卒从间道出不意，大破之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1258668_comment'></div>寨人德公，拔寨与公合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1258668_comment'></div>伸耻其败，攻益力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1258668_comment'></div>会伸破张琪，据濡须城，遣钟乂以十馀万众夹攻，语寨人曰：「为我请王县丞来，否则必屠尔寨」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1258668_comment'></div>公料众寡不敌，将挺身说贼，谕其众曰：「彼围益急，吾势益孤，生路绝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1258668_comment'></div>伸虽粗悍，闻颇知书，可以诚动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1258668_comment'></div>幸而听则免祸，纵见杀犹愈于束手待毙也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1258668_comment'></div>众感泣争止公，公曰：「吾以一身救数万老幼，何畏死」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1258668_comment'></div>即以数十骑出见乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1258668_comment'></div>乂与众贼大惊曰：「公何勇耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1258668_comment'></div>我来无他，盖以公得众心，欲以郡城相委而去尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1258668_comment'></div>公辞不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1258668_comment'></div>乂以矛拥公马而东，日且暮，遂入城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1258668_comment'></div>而张琪复振，与伸战，伸败走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1258668_comment'></div>琪劫公过荻港，令招诱胡避之众，公以计脱归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1258668_comment'></div>时所在盗贼蜂起，杀人如麻，独在胡避者皆得免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1258668_comment'></div>未几丁母忧，镇抚使赵霖以便宜起公摄乡郡，公拊摩疮痍，招集流冗，境内帖然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1258668_comment'></div>有伪为皇侄奉徽宗诏领大元帅者，移檄州郡，公引隽不疑辨戾园事，抵镇抚司，擒送行在所，果得其奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1258668_comment'></div>霖以公守胡避功闻于朝，改承奉郎，就差充镇抚司参谋官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1258668_comment'></div>都督府筑滁州瓦梁堰，为小北海以备敌，委公往视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1258668_comment'></div>公言：「舍江淮天设之险，而积水于敌所不经之地，徒扰民费财尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1258668_comment'></div>遂不复筑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1258668_comment'></div>含山当合肥往来之冲，有狼为害，又委公驱除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1258668_comment'></div>公斋戒入境，狼悉屏迹，人以比宋均渡虎，韩愈徙鳄云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1258668_comment'></div>丁父忧，服除，通判滁州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1258668_comment'></div>时方议和，公移书吏部魏公矼、谏议鲁公统，言辱国非便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1258668_comment'></div>又上疏陈敌有可胜者五，且缴所与二公书，大忤宰相秦桧意，责监南雄州溪塘镇盐税，会赦不果行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1258668_comment'></div>异议者率得重谴，公遂绝意仕进，卜居相山之下，自号相山居士，以诗酒自娱，凡二十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1258668_comment'></div>桧死，起知信阳军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1258668_comment'></div>绍兴三十一年至郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1258668_comment'></div>明年，北人败盟，诏沿边为守备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1258668_comment'></div>公疏言应敌之策，不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1258668_comment'></div>建康都统乞拘沿江舟船，毋泊北岸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1258668_comment'></div>转运司以朝旨移郡，公奏拘老小则失人心，禁商旅则走官课，大将措置乖谬，贻敌笑侮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1258668_comment'></div>鄂州都统乞团结西湖北保甲，遇征行许充本军乡道，公复言：「统帅所谓乡道，是欲驱百姓为先锋耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1258668_comment'></div>朝廷是公言，事俱寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1258668_comment'></div>除就湖北提举常平茶盐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1258668_comment'></div>或言辰、沅、靖三州洞丁习武艺，宜募二千人顺流赴建康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1258668_comment'></div>诏提刑司具舟楫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1258668_comment'></div>公时兼宪事，得符惊曰：「敌未平，岂可复摇远人心」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1258668_comment'></div>奏罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1258668_comment'></div>湖北十四郡常平积粟三十八万，而在鼎州者十五万，陈腐几半，诏以饷荆鄂军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1258668_comment'></div>公曰：「徒费辇运而愈耗折，乞留以为旱备」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1258668_comment'></div>未几，鼎州大旱，公遂发廪以平籴价，取腐坏欠折之数，请于朝而蠲除之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1258668_comment'></div>岁稔，和籴以补其旧，而官吏得逃责，百姓免流殍，二十年积弊悉去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1258668_comment'></div>前提举张公宸语人曰：「王公所为，是吾前日睥睨而不敢为者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1258668_comment'></div>摄鼎州，有僧崇一居桃源，以妖言惑众，公召致狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1258668_comment'></div>民争言僧有神术，治之将不利，公弗听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1258668_comment'></div>狱具，流筠州，卒无能为，乃大诎服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1258668_comment'></div>荆帅乞调鼎、澧、岳乡兵之半同守御，公遗帅书言：「乡兵本以护乡井，岂堪裹甲赴敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1258668_comment'></div>况三郡水旱相仍，安可骚动」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1258668_comment'></div>帅服其言而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1258668_comment'></div>除湖南转运判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1258668_comment'></div>郴寇李金窃发，诸司蒙蔽不以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1258668_comment'></div>公至摄帅事，乞兵于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1258668_comment'></div>贼偶归巢穴，宪遽奏贼就招抚，朝廷信之，追还所遣兵，人情忧惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1258668_comment'></div>公檄宪：「贼若果降，当诣郴公参；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1258668_comment'></div>若自去自来，后必为患」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1258668_comment'></div>檄未至郴，而贼作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1258668_comment'></div>宪惧罪，即报当路以「贼之再发，激于公参之一语」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1258668_comment'></div>言者不察，劾公罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1258668_comment'></div>已而朝廷知其非，宪与二郡守俱镌责，公前枉尽白，而竟不复出矣，遂以朝奉大夫致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1258668_comment'></div>公为人质直刚劲，尚风节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1258668_comment'></div>平居恂恂，气和而色温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1258668_comment'></div>至临大事，区处剖决，多出人意表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1258668_comment'></div>遇人患难，虽雠隙亦极力拯之，不顾家有无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1258668_comment'></div>壮岁入仕，遭时多故，慨然欲以功名自奋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1258668_comment'></div>数上书陈利害，忠义激烈，听者竦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1258668_comment'></div>又以策干丞相赵公鼎、张公浚、吕公颐浩、参政李公光，盖以数公可与共功业者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1258668_comment'></div>其在历阳，料杜充之必败，和州之必变，皆如其言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1258668_comment'></div>和议既成，而公废脱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1258668_comment'></div>守边郡，持使节，当寿皇厉精之初，可以有为，而公已老，亦命也夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1258668_comment'></div>以乾道五年六月朔日终于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1258668_comment'></div>公之将终也，忽语其子曰：「吾衰，久无梦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1258668_comment'></div>畴昔之夜，梦帝召我而命之曰：『以尔有功，当禄其后』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1258668_comment'></div>吾年七十七，死何憾」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1258668_comment'></div>捐馆数日，有白气如练，止舍中，人以为异云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1258668_comment'></div>以其年十月甲申葬于郡城北三十里长冈之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1258668_comment'></div>胡避遗民存者尚众，扶老携幼，遮哭于道，丧车至不得前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1258668_comment'></div>配鲁国夫人孙氏，先公四十二年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1258668_comment'></div>子十人：蘩，奉议郎、签书武冈郡判官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1258668_comment'></div>蘧，迪功郎、郢州长寿尉，皆后公卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1258668_comment'></div>迈，承直郎、监蕲州蕲口镇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1258668_comment'></div>著，迪功郎、监西京岳庙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1258668_comment'></div>𨗨，朝奉郎、通判庐州；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1258668_comment'></div>次即枢密使也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1258668_comment'></div>茹，承务郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1258668_comment'></div>莱，承议郎、前知池州贵池县；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1258668_comment'></div>芾、荀未仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1258668_comment'></div>女六人，适承议郎赵善治、承议郎徐一夔、文林郎许栋、从事郎张汉卿、通直郎万俟侃，幼疾废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1258668_comment'></div>孙男二十人，孙女十九人，曾孙七人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1258668_comment'></div>有文集三十卷，藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1258668_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1258668_comment'></div>读其书可以见公之学，考其始终大节可以知公之心，观其子孙繁衍盛大，又可證天之报施为不诬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1258668_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_133_1258668'>著姓维王，出自太原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1258668_comment'></div>唐季避乱，派分河南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1258668_comment'></div>自河徂淮，累世乃显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1258668_comment'></div>视彼淮水，知其源远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1258668_comment'></div>烈烈太师，以文起家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1258668_comment'></div>与其伯仲，联登隽科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1258668_comment'></div>粤自少年，志出人上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1258668_comment'></div>议论伟然，风节豪壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1258668_comment'></div>始仕邑佐，逢时棘艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1258668_comment'></div>父母之邦，毁于寇残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1258668_comment'></div>鸠集遗黎，依险自保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1258668_comment'></div>耰锄棘矜，以抗群盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1258668_comment'></div>盗环四境，莫婴其锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1258668_comment'></div>稚耋数万，寄命于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1258668_comment'></div>谁谓书生，有谋有勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1258668_comment'></div>云谁厄之，弗究其用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1258668_comment'></div>活人之功，上帝所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1258668_comment'></div>不耀其躬，而后之贻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1258668_comment'></div>是生枢臣，为国硕辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1258668_comment'></div>维垣一品，以贲其墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1258668_comment'></div>长冈之原，公墓在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1258668_comment'></div>植碑勒铭，垂千万年。</div><div id='poem_sentence_154_1258668_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年3月</a>　光宗驾当诣重华宫，复以疾不出，三月，率同列奏言。作品：《乞朝重华宫疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·脱脱等《宋史》卷三八九《尤袤传》据《宋史•光宗本纪》记载（三月丙子，帝朝重华宫，皇后从），该篇当作于是月十九日前，姑系于此。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年3月20日</a>　三月二十日，以礼部尚书兼侍读。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年5月</a>　任礼部尚书，上封事论光宗召浙东总管姜特立。作品：《谏召陈源姜特立封事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·脱脱等《宋史》卷三八九《尤袤传》据《宋史•光宗本纪》记载，五月二十一日召姜特立，留正上疏谏言，不行。六月初三，彭龟年等亦上疏乞寝。则该篇当亦作于其间。）</span><div id='poem_1258622' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258622' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258622?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谏召陈源姜特立封事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258622")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258622_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258622'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258622'>近年以来，给舍、台谏论事，往往不行，如黄裳、郑汝谐事迁延一月，如陈源者奉祠，人情固已惊愕，至姜特立召，尤为骇闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258622_comment'></div>向特立得志之时，昌言台谏皆其门人，窃弄威福，一旦斥去，莫不诵陛下英断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258622_comment'></div>今遽召之，自古去小人甚难，譬除蔓草，犹且复生，况加封植乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258622_comment'></div>若以源、特立有劳，优以外任，或加锡赉，无所不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258622_comment'></div>彼其闲废已久，含愤蓄怨，待此而发，傥复呼之，必将潜引党类，力排异己，朝廷无由安静。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1258622_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　在京，题扬无咎《四清图》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　在京，夏日，王明清来访，与之论史籍及米芾《章圣天临殿记》作品：《与王仲言论史籍》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·王明清《挥麈三录》卷一。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年6月</a>　任礼部尚书，六月，以国事多舛，积忧成疾，上遗奏以劝谏光宗。作品：《遗奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·脱脱等《宋史》卷三八九《尤袤传》）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年6月</a>　任礼部尚书，六月，乞致仕，上遗书以别政府，不报，卒于位。作品：《遗书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·脱脱等《宋史》卷三八九《尤袤传》原作已佚。）</span><br /></div><div class='label1' id='80acee3b13a345efb741b441b8033891_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("80acee3b13a345efb741b441b8033891");'><span id='80acee3b13a345efb741b441b8033891_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1194&endYear=1212')">1194-1212年</a>，卒后1年-卒后19年</div><div id='80acee3b13a345efb741b441b8033891' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1194&endYear=1194')">1194年</a>　转正奉大夫致仕，赠金紫光禄大夫等四官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1212&endYear=1212')">1212年</a>　宋宁宗下诏，赐谥号，曰“文简”<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
泰州
-----detail

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　任泰兴知县，问民疾苦，力除二弊，修筑外城，政绩显著。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年7月11日</a>　七月十一日，任泰兴知县时，以阳楚频易帅守，作诗以讽之。作品：《易帅守》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·徐梦莘《三朝北盟会编》卷二二九。）</span><div id='poem_58606' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58606' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58606?labeling=true' target='_blank'>易帅守</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年7月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_58606")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_58606_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58606'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58606'>维扬五易帅，山阳四易守。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58606'>我来七八月，月月常奔走。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58606'>帑藏忧煎熬，官民困驰骤。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58606'>世态竞趋新，人情盖诣旧。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58606'>如其数移易，是使政纷糅。<div id='poem_sentence_4_58606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_58606'>彼席不得温，设施亦何有。<div id='poem_sentence_5_58606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_58606'>淮南重彫瘵，十室空八九。<div id='poem_sentence_6_58606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_58606'>况复苦将迎，不忍更回首。<div id='poem_sentence_7_58606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_58606'>尝闻古为治，必假岁月久。<div id='poem_sentence_8_58606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_58606'>安得如弈棋，易置翻覆手<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_58606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_58606'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_58606_comment'></div></div><div href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年11月</a>　十一月，坚守泰兴以抗金，为杨抗录抗敌事实。作品：《杨抑之事实》<span class='inlineComment2'>（清·谢旻等《江西通志》卷八五。原作已佚。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>　任泰兴知县，作诗窃哀淮南置山水寨扰民。作品：《淮民谣》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·徐梦莘《三朝北盟会编》卷二四〇。）</span><div id='poem_58609' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58609' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58609?labeling=true' target='_blank'>淮民谣</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_58609")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_58609_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58609'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58609'>东府买舟船，西府买器械。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58609'>问侬欲何为，团结山水寨。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58609'>寨长过我庐，意气甚雄粗。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58609'>青衫两<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_58609", 58609, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>承局</span>，暮夜连<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_58609", 58609, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>勾呼</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58609'><span class='link'
