"Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>椎剥</span>到鸡豕。<div id='poem_sentence_4_58609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_58609'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_58609", 58609, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>供应</span>稍不如，向前受笞箠。<div id='poem_sentence_5_58609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_58609'>驱东复驱西，弃却锄与犁。<div id='poem_sentence_6_58609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_58609'>无钱买刀剑，典尽浑家衣。<div id='poem_sentence_7_58609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_58609'>去年江南荒，趁熟过江北。<div id='poem_sentence_8_58609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_58609'>江北不可往<span class='inlineComment2'>（《诚斋诗话》作住）</span>，江南归未得。<div id='poem_sentence_9_58609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_58609'>父母生我时，教我学耕桑。<div id='poem_sentence_10_58609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_58609'>不识官府严，安能事戎行。<div id='poem_sentence_11_58609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_58609'>执枪不解刺，执弓不能射。<div id='poem_sentence_12_58609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_58609'>团结我何为，徒劳定无益。<div id='poem_sentence_13_58609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_58609'>流离重流离，忍冻复忍饥。<div id='poem_sentence_14_58609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_58609'>谁谓天地宽，一身无所依。<div id='poem_sentence_15_58609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_58609'>淮南丧乱后，安集亦未久。<div id='poem_sentence_16_58609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_58609'>死者积如麻，生者能几口。<div id='poem_sentence_17_58609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_58609'>荒村日西斜，破屋两三家。<div id='poem_sentence_18_58609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_58609'>抚摩力不足，将奈此扰何<span class='inlineComment2'>（同上书卷二四○）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_19_58609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_58609'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_58609_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='a6c5f9ad21294697bd0be638a20a857a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a6c5f9ad21294697bd0be638a20a857a");'><span id='a6c5f9ad21294697bd0be638a20a857a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>，55岁</div><div id='a6c5f9ad21294697bd0be638a20a857a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>　在泰州任提举常平。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='71b5bb5f892647fbbcb6cf1a075657f4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("71b5bb5f892647fbbcb6cf1a075657f4");'><span id='71b5bb5f892647fbbcb6cf1a075657f4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1179')">1178-1179年</a>，55-56岁</div><div id='71b5bb5f892647fbbcb6cf1a075657f4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年12月</a>　在泰州任提举常平，年底与朱熹书函往来，借出程大昌《禹贡论》、吴景轮对札子等文字。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年1月1日</a>　在泰州任提举常平，正月初一，病中吟咏。作品：《己亥元日》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·方回《瀛奎律髓》卷一六。）</span><div id='poem_58594' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58594' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58594?labeling=true' target='_blank'>己亥元日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1179年1月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_58594")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58594_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58594'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58594'>玉历均调岁启端，东风又逐斗杓还。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58594'>萧条门巷经过少，老病腰支拜起难。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58594'>白发但能欺槁项，青春不解驻朱颜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58594'>馀龄有几仍多幸，占得山林一味閒<span class='inlineComment2'>（元方回《瀛奎律髓》卷一六）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58594'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58594_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年1月</a>　在泰州任提举常平，因友人杨万里知常州满，正月除广东提举，故以诗送之。作品：《送提举杨大监解组西归》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·方回《瀛奎律髓》卷二四。）</span><div id='poem_58578' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58578' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58578?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送提举杨大监解组西归<span class='inlineComment2'>（原注：三首取一。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1179年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_58578")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58578_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58578'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58578'>征辕已动不容攀，回首棠阴蔽芾间。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58578'>为郡不知歌舞乐，忧民赢得鬓毛斑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58578'>澄清未展须持节，注想方深便赐环。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58578'>从此相思隔烟水，梦魂飞不到螺山<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58578'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_58578'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_58578_0'>⑴ 原注：首篇有云：“归装见说浑无物，添得新诗数百篇。”即所谓《荆溪集》，传于世。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_58578_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年2月15日</a>　在泰州任提举常平，二月十五日，应邀作文记述魏杞修葺二贤堂事。作品：《二贤堂记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（明·解缙等《永乐大典》卷七二三六。）</span><div id='poem_1258655' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258655' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258655?labeling=true' target='_blank'>二贤堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙六年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258655")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258655_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258655'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258655'>兴旧起废者为政之先务，思贤尚德者风化之本原也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258655_comment'></div>滁阳本淮甸幽僻处，在全盛时不能当一大县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258655_comment'></div>自翰林王公与文忠欧阳公以天下重望，屈临此邦，二公不鄙夷其民，涵养教育，如抚幼稚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258655_comment'></div>方时太平，内外晏然，既不闻田里愁恨之声，因得日与斯民同乐于山巅水涯，因自放于诗酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258655_comment'></div>二公既去，犹眷眷不忘此邦，此邦之人亦怀公之德，如怀其父母，至今如一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258655_comment'></div>虽名公伟儒来守是邦者前后相望，皆不敢与此两人者齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258655_comment'></div>至人诵其诗，家传其像，过其所经行之地，亦必为之动容歛衽，其爱与思之如此其深且久也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258655_comment'></div>始翰林乐其溪山之胜，发于吟咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1258655_comment'></div>迨文忠益疏理泉石，作诸亭于琅琊幽谷两山之间，而自为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1258655_comment'></div>一时名士竞为歌诗，更唱迭和，文献之盛，播于中都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1258655_comment'></div>由是滁之为州，遂名于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1258655_comment'></div>先是滁人绘翰林之像于琅琊山寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1258655_comment'></div>绍圣中，曲阜曾文昭公作二贤堂于郡学西南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1258655_comment'></div>其后邦人别建堂于州城之南七里，岁时必祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1258655_comment'></div>自经兵火，其堂与亭宇焚烁俱尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1258655_comment'></div>其仅能复建者，醉翁一亭而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1258655_comment'></div>淳熙戊戌，寿春魏侯作州之二年，铲敝剔秽，补罅窒隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1258655_comment'></div>威信既行，盗遁奸革，年谷荐稔，帑积盈溢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1258655_comment'></div>暇日登览，访古遗迹，慨然叹曰：「是邦两公之桐乡也，而美迹堙没，祠宇弗治，瞻敬之所，谓斯民何」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1258655_comment'></div>于是因帑积馀财，撙节纤悉，经工庀材，揆之以日，爰即故基，载新祠室，图绘像设，以慰邦人之所以思公者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1258655_comment'></div>凡一泉一石，经昔人之所题品，必表而出之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1258655_comment'></div>既又建丰乐、全声、班春三亭于旧址。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1258655_comment'></div>经始于十一月甲戌，落成于十二月戊申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1258655_comment'></div>向之荒榛，今焉轩楹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1258655_comment'></div>向之瓦砾，今为阶墄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1258655_comment'></div>财取于赢而用不费，役出于卒而民不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1258655_comment'></div>旧观悉还，景物效奇，滁人父老来游宴嬉，瞻望咨嗟，如睹汉仪，如见二公，摩手拊之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1258655_comment'></div>自建炎迄今五十馀年，有废未克举，至侯始尽复而兴起之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1258655_comment'></div>虽若馀事，然变凋瘵创痍之俗为雍容閒暇之邦，其材为可尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1258655_comment'></div>于治民理财之馀，而致思贤尚德之意，其事为可法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1258655_comment'></div>维侯曾祖库部在嘉祐年间再为是州，去文忠公为未远，流风善政犹有存者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1258655_comment'></div>《诗》云：「无念尔祖，聿修厥德」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1258655_comment'></div>在侯有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1258655_comment'></div>侯以书来言曰：「愿有述」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1258655_comment'></div>夫二公之德在民心，虽无此堂，民之思固自若也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1258655_comment'></div>然滁人见其像则恭顺爱敬油然而生，鄙暴之心无自而作，庸有奸其上之令乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1258655_comment'></div>则其为治也易，此前所谓风化之本原者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1258655_comment'></div>惟今州郡，非财赋狱讼所及，漫不复省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1258655_comment'></div>侯独能怀昔贤之高风，葺其祠宇，兴其废迹而致其尊事，是其志非苟然者，固将景行其德而益修其政，其必有以大慰滁人之心者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1258655_comment'></div>予既窃幸托名诸公之次以为荣耀，故乐书其事，又为滁民幸焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1258655_comment'></div>明年二月望日，锡山尤袤记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1258655_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
扬州
-----detail

id='poem_content_58593'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58593'>清风不肯来，烈日不肯暮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58593'>平生山林下，散发颇箕踞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58593'>一官走王事，三伏在道途。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58593'>我非褦襶儿，亦尔困驰骛。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58593'>居然恋俎豆，安得免羁絷。<div id='poem_sentence_4_58593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_58593'>区区竟何营，汩汩此飘寓。<div id='poem_sentence_5_58593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_58593'>渊明应笑人，有底不归去<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='authorDate'>（1162年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_58580")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58580_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58580'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58580'>野色涵空阔，平芜接渺㳽。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58580'>江淮天设险，星斗地分维。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58580'>乔木千年意，沧波万古悲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58580_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_58579' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58579' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58579?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58579_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58579'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58579'>豪杰旧游处，此亭名亦俱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58579'>凄凉谢公堰，浩荡董家湖。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58579'>陈迹成兴废，遗篇今有无。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58579'>登临何限恨，搔首独长吁<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58579'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_58579'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_58579_0'>⑴ 清阿克当阿嘉庆《重修扬州府志》卷三一</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_58579_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
江阴（江阴军）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f94291fb013b487ba61ef59e1a303d1a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f94291fb013b487ba61ef59e1a303d1a");'><span id='f94291fb013b487ba61ef59e1a303d1a_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　注江阴军学教授，需次七年;作诗论及饥民与边兵。作品：《雪》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·方回《瀛奎律髓》卷二一。具体创作时间难以确定，据内容所述，似作于绍兴末江南饥荒之际、宋金议和之前，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_58587' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58587' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_1258666_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258666'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258666'>堂堂钱公，一世之师。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1258666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1258666'>腾实蜚英，自其少时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1258666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1258666'>畴不工文，体弱气萎。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1258666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1258666'>公以道德，养其华滋。<div -----title
临海（台州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8462dfd36d174bc59eaa449ae3ade3a4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8462dfd36d174bc59eaa449ae3ade3a4");'><span id='8462dfd36d174bc59eaa449ae3ade3a4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1176')">1175-1176年</a>，52-53岁</div><div id='8462dfd36d174bc59eaa449ae3ade3a4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年10月3日</a>　十月三日，以承议郎知台州，重修郡城，建节孝巷。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年11月</a>　知台州，十一月，奏请旌表临海县贡士朱柏履妻陈氏。作品：《旌表临海县贡士朱柏履妻陈氏奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·林表民《赤城集》卷一四。原作已佚。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年2月</a>　知台州，正月己未始建霞起堂，二月壬午竣工，有诗。作品：《霞起堂》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·林表民《天台续集别编》卷四。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年2月</a>　知台州，正月己未始建霞起堂，二月壬午竣工，有记。作品：《霞起堂记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·陈耆卿《嘉定赤城志》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_1258652' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258652' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258652?labeling=true' target='_blank'>霞起堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙三年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258652")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258652_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258652'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258652'>双岩堂踞两崖之间，独得地胜，其下面墙，广不寻丈，拥蔽心目，不快人意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258652_comment'></div>予首辟之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258652_comment'></div>墙之外粪壤所潴，乃垦乃夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258652_comment'></div>得旧址焉，撤废亭于射圃，移植其上，榜曰「凝思」，取孙兴公赋所谓「凝思幽岩」者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258652_comment'></div>亭之前有败屋数椽，东向西上，榱栋挠折，隅奥庳仄，乃改创为堂，三楹南乡，与静镇堂相直，因名曰「霞起」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258652_comment'></div>由双岩而望静镇，直若引绳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258652_comment'></div>其外绕以回廊，上连参云，以为风雨游观之备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258652_comment'></div>爰植美竹，以经纬之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1258652_comment'></div>于是堂成而胜益奇，前所未睹，披豁呈露，天若开而明，地若广而敞，景物若增益而富。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1258652_comment'></div>晨烟夕霏，万化千变，近峰远岭，閒见层出，皆可不出檐庑而尽得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1258652_comment'></div>噫，是亦足以广心志，荡尘垢，而非苟以为娱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1258652_comment'></div>惟此邦灵山所宅，昔号胜处，自经大旱，遂成陋邦，而山川之秀，不异今昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1258652_comment'></div>或谓予当单乏之际，顾为此不急之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1258652_comment'></div>然取材于旧，课工于卒，不市一木，不役一民，而使隘者敞，窒者通，弊者新，则亦何害于政哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1258652_comment'></div>第废材不足以支久，尚能十稔，若其革而鼎之，以俟后之君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1258652_comment'></div>始役于淳熙三年正月己未，成于二月壬午。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1258652_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>　知台州，立乐山堂，有诗。作品：《乐山堂》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·林表民《天台续集别编》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_58595' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58595' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58595?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乐山堂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_58595")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_58595_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58595'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58595'>草堂有遗基，榛莽岁月久。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58595'>我来始经葺，挹翠开户牖。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58595'>群山供啸傲，万象皆奔走。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58595'>所以名乐山，欲企仁者寿。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58595'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58595_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>　知台州，重建玉霄亭，有诗。作品：《玉霄亭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·林表民《天台续集别编》卷四。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>　知台州，重建玉霄亭，有记。作品：《玉霄亭柱记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·陈耆卿《嘉定赤城志》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_1258653' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258653' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258653?labeling=true' target='_blank'>玉霄亭柱记</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258653")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258653_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258653'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258653'>台州南、西、北三面逼山，独东望诸峰差远，云烟空濛，外际溟海，蓬莱方丈，想见其处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258653_comment'></div>旧有小亭在子城之上，绍兴丁卯，南丰曾使君谹父创建，更名玉霄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258653_comment'></div>距今三十年，摧败倾圮，岌嶪欲压。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258653_comment'></div>其下昔有茂林脩竹，今皆剪伐，错为民居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258653_comment'></div>溷圊罗列，污秽喧嚣，游者叹息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258653_comment'></div>余乃披剃蠲疏，载芟载除，四为缭墙以限外涂，下建石柱，上跨飞阁，出亭之外，又有六尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258653_comment'></div>凡楹栋榱桷之朽挠，叠瓴级甓之缺折，丹黄粉漆之陊剥，皆易而新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258653_comment'></div>方连周陆，可倚可眺，晨揖灏气，夕延素月，山川城郭，尽在几席之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1258653_comment'></div>凭栏四望，叠嶂环绕，手挥丝桐，目送飞鸿，飘飘乎如乘云御风，身在物表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1258653_comment'></div>州之宴游，于是为胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1258653_comment'></div>乃刻亭柱以纪岁月云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1258653_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>　知台州，重建清平阁，有诗。作品：《清平阁》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·林表民《天台续集别编》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_58599' id='poem_sentence_1_58592_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58592'>别来望远凭谁寄，老去寻春只恐迟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58592_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58592'>把酒问花花解语，定应催促要新诗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58592_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58592'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58592_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_58591' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58591' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58591?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58591'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58591'>立马黄昏绕曲池，几回踏雪问南枝。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58591'>不应春到花犹未，定恐寒侵力不支。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58591'>陇上已惊传信晚，樽前只想<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_3_58591'>临风不语空归去，独立无憀自咏诗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58591'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_58590_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58590'>无钱可办罗浮醉，报答春光只有诗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58590_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年2月15日</a>　知台州，二月十五日，题王厚之藏《兰亭帖》作品：《题王顺伯第二本》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·桑世昌《兰亭考》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1258639' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258639' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258639?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题王顺伯第二本</a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年2月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258639")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258639_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258639'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258639'>唐文皇既得《脩禊叙》，命赵模、韩道政、诸葛桢、冯承素拓赐诸王近臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258639_comment'></div>虞、褚、欧阳各有临迹，至今不知几本，而独贵定武刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258639_comment'></div>顺伯诸本皆佳，顾以字肥而不刓者为定武，则与余所见特异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258639_comment'></div>杨柽伯时有薛道祖亲签题一本正肥，云是唐古本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258639_comment'></div>平生所见前辈所跋定武本，皆有依据，一毕少董家赐本，一蒋丞相家米元章诸人跋本，一张文潜家王岐公跋本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258639_comment'></div>最后见澄江吕氏舒王所跋，与此本无毫发异，其刓缺处正同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258639_comment'></div>益信山谷所谓肥不剩肉，瘦不露骨者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258639_comment'></div>后有识者，当赏余之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1258639_comment'></div>淳熙四年仲春望日，尤袤题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1258639_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年</a>　知台州，游天庆观，有记。作品：《昊天殿记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·陈耆卿《嘉定赤城志》卷二三。其在台州两年有余，是岁任满，姑系该事于此。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年</a>　知台州，欲修纂台州地方志，未成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年</a>　知台州，起释处良领紫櫜。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年</a>　知台州，遣书礼徐庭筠。作品：《与徐季节先生书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·脱脱等《宋史》卷四五九《徐中行传》该篇作于尤袤知台州期间，是岁任满，姑系于此;原作已佚。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年</a>　得唐人贺知章草书帖，刻置天台郡斋。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年</a>　知台州，定业院新铸成铜钟，应王铢之邀而作记。作品：《定业院新铸铜钟记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（尤桐《锡山尤氏丛刊·甲集》该篇当作于尤袤知台州期间，是岁任满，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_1258661' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258661' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258661?labeling=true' target='_blank'>定业院新铸铜钟记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258661")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258661_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258661'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258661'>临海之义诚白岩山定业院，乃近故参知政事、资政殿大学士襄阳王敏肃公墓侧之精蓝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258661_comment'></div>建于唐光启二年，其钟铸于乾宁四载，岁久钟坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258661_comment'></div>今主僧景猷与其徒景宗等募缘鸠工，将新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258661_comment'></div>按旧钟具列台州刺史司空杜雄等名衔，殆今三百有馀年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258661_comment'></div>将改铸之月，敏肃公之仲子通直郎、主管建昌军仙都观铢来请曰：「钟旧有州主姓氏，今不可以无述」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258661_comment'></div>因求记焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1258661_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1178')">1177-1178年</a>　台州任满，十二月十三日，除淮南东路提举常平茶盐。作品：《别林景思》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·杨万里《诚斋集》卷九九。尤袤居官三衢的具体时间难以确定，据其浙东任官之下限，姑系于此。）</span>《台州四诗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·林表民《天台续集别编》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_58570' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58570' 贵池

id='poem_title_1258656' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258656?labeling=true' target='_blank'>报恩光孝寺僧堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙六年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258656")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258656_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258656'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258656'>淳熙三年秋九月，故参政观文钱公施其私财于台州报恩光孝禅寺，复建僧堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258656_comment'></div>明年九月十二日经始，后十五日而公薨，又明年六月二日堂成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258656_comment'></div>中为大屋七閒，高七寻，其广四十有二尺，其深十寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258656_comment'></div>前列脩廊，后布广庑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258656_comment'></div>其楹高与广皆如其堂之数，而崇深杀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258656_comment'></div>贯三挟廊，为二井匽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258656_comment'></div>凡为屋之楹，大小二十有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258656_comment'></div>规模雄壮，悉倍于旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1258656_comment'></div>公之孙承议郎、前知处州军州事象祖题其榜曰「选佛」，合道俗以落之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1258656_comment'></div>又明年，长老惟禋命其徒了性持书求文于锡山尤袤，而记之曰：天台为邦，仙圣所游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1258656_comment'></div>佛法之盛，冠于东州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1258656_comment'></div>有大丛林，旧名景德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1258656_comment'></div>众妙庄严，近在城域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1258656_comment'></div>政和之初，赐额天宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1258656_comment'></div>绍兴之閒，始易今名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1258656_comment'></div>是为祐陵，邀福之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1258656_comment'></div>列屋千楹，有众万指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1258656_comment'></div>乾道癸巳，郁攸扇灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1258656_comment'></div>绀壁穹堂，化为飞灰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1258656_comment'></div>时大比丘，德光长老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1258656_comment'></div>立志坚忍，誓必再造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1258656_comment'></div>乃泛扁舟，浮海而南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1258656_comment'></div>持钵于泉，半载乃还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1258656_comment'></div>憔悴辛勤，寸累铢积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1258656_comment'></div>乃建众寮，乃营丈室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1258656_comment'></div>规创后壁，架虚凿空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1258656_comment'></div>商工度材，施者景从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1258656_comment'></div>惟光之名，进于帝听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1258656_comment'></div>有诏自天，命主灵隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1258656_comment'></div>袤时假守，睹是胜因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1258656_comment'></div>求继光后，实难其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1258656_comment'></div>万口一词，曰有权可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1258656_comment'></div>乃屈致之，权不拒我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1258656_comment'></div>于煨烬中，启大法筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1258656_comment'></div>远近皈依，辐辏骈阗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1258656_comment'></div>宝殿迄成，材从空堕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1258656_comment'></div>权未尝为，不起于坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1258656_comment'></div>有大檀施，观文公钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1258656_comment'></div>与是比丘，有大因缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1258656_comment'></div>私自念言，安聚衲子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1258656_comment'></div>以有伽蓝，为一大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1258656_comment'></div>尊师所在，龙象骏奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1258656_comment'></div>四方学徒，其来如云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1258656_comment'></div>而此僧堂，独未建立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1258656_comment'></div>起寺之废，莫此为急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1258656_comment'></div>我当布施，为众生先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1258656_comment'></div>捐三百万，于指顾閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1258656_comment'></div>公之视财，如视壤土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1258656_comment'></div>我无所施，随取而予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1258656_comment'></div>权之受施，如谷遇风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1258656_comment'></div>我无所受，有来则容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1258656_comment'></div>权谓其徒，监寺了性：「汝敏而勤，命总其政」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1258656_comment'></div>性亦受令，奔走后先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1258656_comment'></div>陶瓦成山，伐木蔽川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1258656_comment'></div>权来权藏，四众嗟惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1258656_comment'></div>予邀惟禋，嗣其法席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1258656_comment'></div>禋之始来，众曰艰哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1258656_comment'></div>禋来一年，众志允谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1258656_comment'></div>巧者献伎，壮者出力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1258656_comment'></div>涓日亢徒，并举百役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1258656_comment'></div>乃立斯堂，其大七楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1258656_comment'></div>高广深邃，寒温暑清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1258656_comment'></div>前荣后庑，两倍其数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1258656_comment'></div>寝食有位，宴息有所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1258656_comment'></div>伟哉斯堂，肇自钱公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1258656_comment'></div>不逮其成，而公已终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1258656_comment'></div>惟公有孙，衔训嗣事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1258656_comment'></div>爰饰几榻，至于涂塈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1258656_comment'></div>斋鼓粥鱼，隐隐隆隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1258656_comment'></div>摄齐升堂，肃肃雍雍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1258656_comment'></div>旧观复还，百废具举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1258656_comment'></div>如聩得听，若瞽而睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1258656_comment'></div>数有成坏，时有废兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1258656_comment'></div>法力愿力，为无不成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1258656_comment'></div>惟三比丘，与二居士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1258656_comment'></div>往昔灵山，并受佛记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1258656_comment'></div>作此胜事，刹那顷中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1258656_comment'></div>化瓦砾场，为梵帝宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1258656_comment'></div>咨汝大众，享此安逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1258656_comment'></div>云何脩行，报此恩德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1258656_comment'></div>当念作者，法力宏深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1258656_comment'></div>勇猛精进，无起退心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1258656_comment'></div>当念施者，愿力坚重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1258656_comment'></div>量彼来处，无妄受用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1258656_comment'></div>惟上祖师，穴处岩居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1258656_comment'></div>今汝不然，夏屋渠渠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1258656_comment'></div>惟上祖师，行乞取足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1258656_comment'></div>今汝不然，饱饭果腹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1258656_comment'></div>广席连床，窗户明虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1258656_comment'></div>心境洞然，万法一如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1258656_comment'></div>卧具巾单，随用无乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1258656_comment'></div>困歇饥餐，莫非妙法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1258656_comment'></div>汝若一念，證常寂光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1258656_comment'></div>华严境界，即是此堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1258656_comment'></div>汝若不断，五欲三毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1258656_comment'></div>当知此堂，即是地狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1258656_comment'></div>巾山崇崇，与堂无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1258656_comment'></div>我为斯文，相其鼓钟。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_97_1258656'></div><div id='poem_sentence_97_1258656_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年</a>　在池州任提举常平，秋，应临海令彭仲刚之邀而作文。作品：《临海县重建县治记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·林表民《赤城集》卷三。据文中所述，该篇当作于是年秋县治重新落成之际。）</span><div id='poem_1258657' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258657' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258657?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临海县重建县治记</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙六年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258657")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258657_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258657'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258657'>乾道癸巳秋九月，临海居民不戒于火，滥烂扇延，以及县治，燔爇俱尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258657_comment'></div>当官者因陋就简，仅建三椽于煨烬之中，以听狱讼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258657_comment'></div>吏民无所托足，案牍无所栖列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258657_comment'></div>一遇风雨，则沾渍暴露，叫呼欢呶，讼牒计簿散匿吏胥之家，最易甲乙，莫可质考，县日以不理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258657_comment'></div>后三年，予来为州，有意兴之，而无与任其责者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258657_comment'></div>淳熙丁酉秋，永嘉彭君仲刚来主县事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258657_comment'></div>予闻彭君旧矣，心固望其有为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258657_comment'></div>彭乃言曰：「夫环百里之地而为之长，聚万室之众而听其令，民社所寄，视古子男。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1258657_comment'></div>治必有所，一邑之条教于是乎出，而司存弗备，亡以施政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1258657_comment'></div>废之当举，舍此孰先？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1258657_comment'></div>然役大用夥，非受命于郡，则令不得擅，敢以为请」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1258657_comment'></div>予乃畀钱三十万，使营度之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1258657_comment'></div>是冬，予罢官归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1258657_comment'></div>踰年，则彭以书来告成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1258657_comment'></div>外为重门，以严启闭，上建层楼，以敛敕书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1258657_comment'></div>治事有厅，燕居有室，翼以脩廊，挟以外庑，吏直宾次，环列有序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1258657_comment'></div>奥者为藏，爽者为狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1258657_comment'></div>为亭于大门之外，以班诏令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1258657_comment'></div>为阁于东庑之上，以藏案牍，为堂为斋为轩，以备宴休游息之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1258657_comment'></div>下至于庖湢之所，微至于什器之末，杂至于丹雘甃甓之事，纤悉毕具，规模坚壮，工用精密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1258657_comment'></div>总为屋八十有一楹，中凿五池，潴水为备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1258657_comment'></div>复以其馀力，建丞簿之舍而新社稷之坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1258657_comment'></div>乡之荆榛瓦砾之场，今乃为高明宏丽之观，民始识有官府之严而称其所以为邑大夫之居者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1258657_comment'></div>问其经费之所出，则曰未尝巧取而奇敛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1258657_comment'></div>凡财之隐于吏而亡籍，木之讼于官而愿献者，悉取而拘之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1258657_comment'></div>钩校畸赢，积累铢寸，故费广而不阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1258657_comment'></div>问其工役之次第，则曰未尝厉民而强使也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1258657_comment'></div>籍境内之为工者若干，官出僦庸，率如其私之直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1258657_comment'></div>居处饮食，先为规画，使极安便，率旬有五日而迭休之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1258657_comment'></div>其用夫止及于附邑之三乡，家止一人，人役三日，番无过十夫，而亦与之庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1258657_comment'></div>省督工程，无苟简怠惰之患；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1258657_comment'></div>谨视给散，无稽留脧削之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1258657_comment'></div>民之与官为市为役者，若私家然，故役大而不扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1258657_comment'></div>盖经始于丁酉之冬，而落成于己亥之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1258657_comment'></div>问其所以久，则曰：不敢仓卒而趣办也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1258657_comment'></div>作于农隙而弗夺其时，休其力而弗尽其用，慰谕其勤而策其不勉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1258657_comment'></div>民咸劝趋，故功成而不劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1258657_comment'></div>夫聚财有方，用民有节，举事有渐，顾何往而不济哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1258657_comment'></div>予尝谓今之士莫难于为邑，弱者不足以有为，而健者或以病民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1258657_comment'></div>幸而得强弱之中，则积负困之，奸民挠之，欲兴事造业，有其志而不克成者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1258657_comment'></div>又幸而不为积负之所困，奸民之所挠，而在上者或不察，不得自展其才者亦多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1258657_comment'></div>当君之始至，赋乱政庬，隐户移税，弗可究诘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1258657_comment'></div>乃考质剂而正疆理，逋租匿役，披露首服，吏奸民瘼，检柅济理，田野欢呼，讼日以简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1258657_comment'></div>故能不困于积负，不挠于奸民，不抑于当路，而兴旧起废，不扰而集，非庶几于古之所谓循吏者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1258657_comment'></div>夫裒聚赢羡于单乏之馀，可以观俭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1258657_comment'></div>谨用民力于偪仄之中，可以观仁，积累工役于迟久之后，可以观智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1258657_comment'></div>是皆足以为吏法，而不可使之无传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1258657_comment'></div>予既嘉彭君之有成，而因其请，故遂著其实，使后之人得以考而法之，非以谕彭君也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_47_1258657_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年10月</a>　在池州任提举常平，十月，拟刻《昭明文选》，袁说友相与规度费用。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年11月13日</a>　在池州任提举常平，应朱熹之邀作文。作品：《五贤祠记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（尤桐《锡山尤氏丛刊·甲集》）</span><div id='poem_1258658' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258658' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258658?labeling=true' target='_blank'>五贤祠记</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙六年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258658")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258658_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258658'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258658'>南康使君朱侯熹下车之初，先即学宫立濂溪周先生与二程夫子之祠于学之西序，属其友张栻敬夫为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258658_comment'></div>则又考古今士之居是邦者，得五人，曰晋靖节徵士陶公，本朝西涧居士刘公，兵部尚书李公，谏议忠肃陈公，与西涧之子秘丞，复立祠于学之东序，而俾愚记之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258658_comment'></div>愚闻古之乡先生殁则祭于社，所以崇教化励风俗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258658_comment'></div>史称靖节为柴桑人，而《图经》以为徙居栗里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258658_comment'></div>渊明《还旧居诗》云：「畴昔家上京」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258658_comment'></div>上京在今都城外十里，而栗里源去郡一舍，《传》与《集》皆不载其尝徙于此，而独见颜鲁公之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258658_comment'></div>然南康故为浔阳属邑，则渊明盖此邦之人不疑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258658_comment'></div>刘公居筠阳，慕庐山之胜而徙焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1258658_comment'></div>方天圣、明道间，士之怀材抱道者靡不奋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1258658_comment'></div>公高气盖世，仕州县一不合意，即挂冠归隐，结庐于净隐寺之西涧，欧阳文忠公赋《庐山高》以美之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1258658_comment'></div>道原之节，不减其父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1258658_comment'></div>熙宁中，用事者欲挽以自助，掉臂不顾，若将浼焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1258658_comment'></div>求为南康酒官，以便亲养，遂终其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1258658_comment'></div>李尚书生郡之建昌，少时读书五老峰下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1258658_comment'></div>当条例司初建时，公与程明道俱为属，不深辞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1258658_comment'></div>及青苗、均输之议出，力起而争之，章十数上，由是去国十五年，晚方召还，旋乞外补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1258658_comment'></div>其山房与苏长公之记，今尚亡恙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1258658_comment'></div>陈谏议家延平，坐诋蔡氏连斥，稍复官奉祠，自九江来居此邦，盖无几时，而此邦之人尊而敬之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1258658_comment'></div>是五人者，其出处虽不同，其名节大略相似，其所以扶世立教，其归一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1258658_comment'></div>渊明居乱世，耻事二姓，故无意于仕，而不失其高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1258658_comment'></div>刘公父子生治世，自信所守，故有意于隐，而不害其为介。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1258658_comment'></div>李尚书出处进退，终始不渝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1258658_comment'></div>陈忠肃颠踣撼顿，死而不悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1258658_comment'></div>所谓奋乎百世之上，使百世之下闻者兴起，非此五人者而谁欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1258658_comment'></div>今侯负天下重名，特起为二千石，不鄙其民，手摩抚之，民亦安其清静，相戒以毋犯太守条教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1258658_comment'></div>侯知邦人之可与为善，思有以风厉鼓发，乃祠是五人者，使凡游乎乡校而睹其遗像，其善者跃然而喜，常若五君子之诱之也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1258658_comment'></div>其不善者惕然而惧，常若五君子之临之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1258658_comment'></div>然礼义兴行而风俗淳厚，将不在兹乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1258658_comment'></div>抑尝谓古者道化行于乡党之间，必有一乡之善士为之表率，生则师尊之，死则祠祭之，故人有所慕而为善，有所畏而不为恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1258658_comment'></div>其师友渊源，薰陶渐渍，愈久而愈可爱慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1258658_comment'></div>自先王之教不明，而隆师尊友之义废，斯人气质斲丧几尽，后生晚学不复识前辈典型，耳濡目染，安于末路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1258658_comment'></div>而为政者，大抵汩没于财赋狱讼之间，事之关于风教，则一切指为迂阔，漫不复议，故无以感发斯人之善心而阴消其傲慢之气，变易其鄙薄之习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1258658_comment'></div>方且操其堤防笼络之具，形驱而势格之，奸愈不胜，俗日益靡，则诿曰民不如古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1258658_comment'></div>呜呼，民之不如古，无乃吏之所以为教者非欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1258658_comment'></div>余于侯之所为独有感也，故并书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1258658_comment'></div>若夫五君子之所行，见于史，此不尽著，特著其所以立祠之意云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1258658_comment'></div>淳熙己亥仲冬丁丑，晋陵尤袤记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1258658_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年</a>　在池州任提举常平，应朱熹之邀作诗。作品：《刘屯田墓壮节亭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·方回《瀛奎律髓》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_58566' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58566' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58566?labeling=true' target='_blank'>刘屯田墓壮节亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1179年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_58566")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58566_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58566'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58566'>西涧当年卜考槃，便于神武挂衣冠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58566'>后生无复知前辈，故老犹能说长官。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58566'>三尺荒坟埋玉冷，百年壮节倚天寒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58566'>表章赖有群贤力，谁把生刍奠酒盘<span class='inlineComment2'>（同上书卷二八）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58566'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58566_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年</a>　在池州任提举常平，为友人毛幵撰墓志铭。作品：《毛平仲墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·陈振孙《直斋书录解题》卷一八。具体时间难以确定，据毛氏大约卒年，姑系于此。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年</a>　在池州任提举常平，序友人毛幵文集。作品：《〈樵隐集〉序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·陈振孙《直斋书录解题》卷一八。具体时间难以确定，据毛氏大约卒年，姑系于此。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年2月8日</a>　在池州任提举常平，二月八日，跋《山海经》作品：《〈山海经〉跋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（明·毛扆校宋本《山海经》附。）</span><div id='poem_1258642' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258642' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258642?labeling=true' target='_blank'>山海经跋</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙七年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258642")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258642_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258642'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258642'>《山海经》十八篇，世云夏禹为之，非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258642_comment'></div>其间或㨙启及有穷后羿之事，汉儒云翳为之，亦非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258642_comment'></div>然屈原《离骚经》多摘取其事，则其为先秦书不疑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258642_comment'></div>是书所言，多荒忽诞谩，若不可信，故世君子以为六合之外，圣人之所不论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258642_comment'></div>以予观之，则亦无足疑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258642_comment'></div>方天地未奠之初，彝伦故未始有序也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258642_comment'></div>兽蹄鸟迹之道交于中国，则人与禽兽未能有别也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258642_comment'></div>夫性命之未得其正，则赋形于天者不能一定，其诡异固宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1258642_comment'></div>逮夫天尊地卑而乾坤定，于是手持足蹈以为人，戴角傅翼以为鸟兽，类聚群分，始能有以自别，而圣人者出而君长之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1258642_comment'></div>以为人者，不特其形之如是也，又从而制为仁义礼乐，以为之尸文，俾之自别于禽兽，而人益尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1258642_comment'></div>故夫人者，其初亦天地之一物而特灵者耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1258642_comment'></div>自今观之，凡若遂言之所言，故多怪诞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1258642_comment'></div>自古观之，则理固有是而不足疑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1258642_comment'></div>是书所载，自开辟数千万年，遐方异域，不可诘知之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1258642_comment'></div>盖自《禹贡》职方氏之外，其辨山川草木鸟兽所出，莫备于此书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1258642_comment'></div>又秦汉学者多引《山海经》，兹固益可信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1258642_comment'></div>古书得存于今，如是者鲜矣，则岂不可贵且重乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1258642_comment'></div>始予得京都旧印本三卷，颇疏略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1258642_comment'></div>继得《道藏》本，《南山》、《东山经》各自为一卷，《西山》、《北山》各分为上、下两卷，《中山》为上、中、下三卷，别以《中山东、北》为一卷，《海外南》、《海外东、北》、《海内西、南》、《海内东、北《、》大荒东、南》、《大荒西》、《大荒北》、《海内经》，总为十八卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1258642_comment'></div>虽编简号为均一，而篇目错乱不齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1258642_comment'></div>晚得刘歆所定书，其《南》、《西》、《北》、《东》及《中山》号五藏经，为五篇，其文最多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1258642_comment'></div>《海内》、《海外》、《大荒》三经，南西北东各一篇，并《海内经》一篇，亦总十八篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1258642_comment'></div>多者十馀简，少者三二简，虽若卷帙不均，而篇次整比最古，遂为定本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1258642_comment'></div>予自绍兴辛未至今，垂三十年，所见无虑十数本，参校得失，于是稍无舛讹，可缮写。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1258642_comment'></div>其卷后，或题建平元年四月丙戌待诏太常属臣望校治，侍中光禄勋臣龚、侍中奉车都尉光禄大夫臣秀领主省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1258642_comment'></div>建平实汉哀帝年号，是岁刘歆以欲应图谶，始改名秀，而龚则王龚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1258642_comment'></div>哀帝时朝臣有两名望者，一则丁望，一则蟜望，而此疑为丁望云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1258642_comment'></div>淳熙庚子仲春八日，梁溪尤袤题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1258642_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>　在池州任提举常平，夏日，大旱，赈灾。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>　增刻洪适《隶续》二卷于江东仓台以成二十一卷全书，而辇其板归之越。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>　在池州任提举常平，寄送《五贤祠记》与朱熹，其刻印后转寄吕祖谦。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>　在池州任提举常平，李焘荐任史官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>　在池州任提举常平，作文纪念毕士安等三人。作品：《思贤堂三赞》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·林表民《赤城集》卷八。）</span><br /></div><div class='label1' id='eafc0c3ccaeb45cbb219f483bccb574a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("eafc0c3ccaeb45cbb219f483bccb574a");'><span id='eafc0c3ccaeb45cbb219f483bccb574a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年</a>，58岁</div><div id='eafc0c3ccaeb45cbb219f483bccb574a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年2月15日</a>　在池州任提举常平，二月十五日，跋米元晖《潇湘图卷》作品：《跋米元晖〈潇湘图卷〉》<span class='inlineComment2'>（明·赵琦美《赵氏铁网珊瑚》卷一一。据赵琦美《赵氏铁网珊瑚》卷一一《潇湘图考》的记载，尤袤时通判池州。）</span><div id='poem_1258643' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258643' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258643?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋米元晖潇湘图卷</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙八年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258643")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258643_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258643'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258643'>蔡天启作《米襄阳墓志》，言元符初，进其子所画《万里长江图》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258643_comment'></div>时元晖年尚少，其小笔已知名当世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258643_comment'></div>方此老无恙时，诸公贵人求索者日填门，不胜厌苦，往往多令门下士仿作，而亲识元晖二字于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258643_comment'></div>尝自言：「遇合作处，浑然天成，荐为之不复相似」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258643_comment'></div>此卷寂寥简短，不过数笔，而浅深浓淡，姿态横生，使人应接不暇，盖是其得意笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258643_comment'></div>自其云亡，画益难得，矧题识皆一时名胜之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258643_comment'></div>终日把玩，不能去手也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258643_comment'></div>淳熙辛丑二月中休，梁溪尤袤题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1258643_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年2月15日</a>　在池州任提举常平，二月十五日，序《朱逢年诗集》作品：《朱逢年诗集序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·朱槔《玉澜集》卷末附。）</span><div id='poem_1258644' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258644' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258644?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朱逢年诗集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙八年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258644")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258644_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258644'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258644'>英伟豪杰之士，生必有所自来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258644_comment'></div>故其亡也，决不泯泯与草木俱腐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258644_comment'></div>观玉澜先生之集，顾不异哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258644_comment'></div>夫得则喜，失则悲，有所不平则怨刺，此诗人之情也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258644_comment'></div>惟深于道者不然，无人而不自得，先生近之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258644_comment'></div>先生少有轶材，自负其长，不肯随俗俯仰，厄穷踸踔，有人所难堪，而其节愈厉，其气愈高，其诗閒暇，略不见悲伤憔悴之态。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258644_comment'></div>其视富贵利达真糠秕土苴尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258644_comment'></div>《春风》一篇，雍容广大，有圣门舞雩气象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1258644_comment'></div>《感事》三篇，慨然见经世之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1258644_comment'></div>自作《挽歌词》，齐得丧，一死生，直欲友渊明于千载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1258644_comment'></div>至所谓「自我识兴废，于天无怨尤」，非深于道者能如是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1258644_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1258644_comment'></div>以先生之才，使其作于声诗，荐之郊庙，发其所蕴，措诸事业，何愧古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1258644_comment'></div>百不一售，使后世所以知公者，独此数十诗而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1258644_comment'></div>悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1258644_comment'></div>先生有兄曰韦斋，白首郎潜，不究大用，人以为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1258644_comment'></div>其诗凌厉高古，有建安七子之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1258644_comment'></div>韦斋之子南康使君，今又以道学倡，其诗源远而流长，信矣哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1258644_comment'></div>淳熙辛丑仲春望日，梁溪尤袤敬跋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1258644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1258644'><span class='label'>按：</span>《玉澜集》卷末，四部丛刊续编本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1258644_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年2月18日</a>　在池州任提举常平，二月十八日，题米元晖《潇湘图》作品：《题米元晖〈潇湘图〉二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（明·赵琦美《赵氏铁网珊瑚》卷一一。）</span><div id='poem_58612' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58612' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58612?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题米元晖潇湘图二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1181年2月18日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_58612")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>六言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58612_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58612'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58612'>万里江天杳霭，一村烟树微茫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58612'>只欠孤篷听雨，恍如身在潇湘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58612'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_58612_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_58611' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58611' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58611?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1181年2月18日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>六言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58611_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58611'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58611'>淡淡晴山横雾，茫茫远水平沙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58611_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58611'>安得绿蓑青笠，往来泛宅浮家<span class='inlineComment2'>（明赵琦美《赵氏铁网珊瑚》卷三）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58611_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58611'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_58611_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年3月3日</a>　在池州任提举常平，三月初三，刻《昭明文选》毕，有跋。作品：《〈昭明文选〉跋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋本《文选》卷末。）</span><div id='poem_1258645' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258645' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258645?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭明文选跋</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙八年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258645")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258645_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258645'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258645'>贵池在萧梁时实为昭明太子封邑，血食千载，威灵赫然，水旱疾疫，无祷不应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258645_comment'></div>庙有文选阁，宏丽壮伟，而独无是书之板，盖缺典也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258645_comment'></div>往岁邦人尝欲募众力为之，不成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258645_comment'></div>今是书流传于世，皆是五臣注本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258645_comment'></div>五臣特训释旨意，多不原用事所出，独李善淹贯该洽，号为精详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258645_comment'></div>虽四明、赣上各尝刊勒，往往裁节语句，可恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258645_comment'></div>袤因以俸馀锓木，会池阳袁使君助其费，郡文学周之纲督其役，踰年乃克成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258645_comment'></div>既摹本藏之阁上，以其板置之学宫，以慰邦人所以尊事昭明之意云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1258645_comment'></div>淳熙辛丑上巳日，晋陵尤袤题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1258645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1258645'><span class='label'>按：</span>《梁溪遗稿》文钞补编。又见中华书局影印宋刻本《文选》卷末。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1258645_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年闰3月27日</a>　在池州任提举常平，因友人朱熹南康任满，闰三月二十七日，除江西提刑，去郡归，故以诗送之。作品：《送晦庵南归》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·方回《瀛奎律髓》卷二四。）</span><div id='poem_58577' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58577' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58577?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送晦庵南归</a><span class='authorDate'>（1181年闰3月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_58577")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58577_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58577'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58577'>二年摩手抚疮痍，恩与庐山五老齐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58577'>合侍玉皇香案侧，却持华节大江西。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58577'>鼎新白鹿诸生学，筑就长虹万丈堤。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58577'>待哺饥民偏恋德，老翁犹作小儿啼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58577'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58577_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年</a>　在池州任提举常平，与袁说友共同刊刻《文选双字》、《昭明文集》等书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年6月</a>　在池州任提举常平，六月，赠送莲花与袁说友，并有文字记之。作品：《寄赠袁知州双莲》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·袁说友《东塘集》卷六。原作已佚。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年6月</a>　六月，刻洪适《隶释》五十卷于秋浦。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
句容
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d2ff229f1faf41d4a2c5bec2d486285e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d2ff229f1faf41d4a2c5bec2d486285e");'><span id='d2ff229f1faf41d4a2c5bec2d486285e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>，57岁</div><div id='d2ff229f1faf41d4a2c5bec2d486285e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年12月29日</a>　十二月二十九日，游茅山，有诗。作品：《庚子岁除前一日游茅山》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·刘大彬《茅山志》卷一五。）</span><div id='poem_58605' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58605' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58605?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庚子岁除前一日游茅山</a><span class='authorDate'>（1180年12月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_58605")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_58605_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58605'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58605'>犯寒出行遇<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑作迈）</span>，值此岁云除。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58605'>刚风驾飙轮，送我游清都。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58605'>华阳第八天，仙圣之所居。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58605'>洞门劣容人，中宽如室庐。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58605'>横前大溪水，于焉限尘区。<div id='poem_sentence_4_58605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_58605'>其右万石林，错落空翠图。<div id='poem_sentence_5_58605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_58605'>茅庵著深秀，细路缘崎岖。<div id='poem_sentence_6_58605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_58605'>幽泉见客喜，颇亦类逃虚。<div id='poem_sentence_7_58605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_58605'>山深日易曛，捷径趋元符<span class='inlineComment2'>（符字与后赤城符重韵）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_58605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_58605'>琳宫照金碧，天籁鸣笙竽。<div id='poem_sentence_9_58605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_58605'>侧睨白云峰，前瞻赤沙湖。<div id='poem_sentence_10_58605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_58605'>金坛耸百丈，阴洞通七途。<div id='poem_sentence_11_58605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_58605'>俯视人间世，扰扰真虫蛆。<div id='poem_sentence_12_58605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_58605'>蚤以凡陋质，忝分赤城符。<div id='poem_sentence_13_58605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_58605'>岂悟夙昔缘，复造神灵墟。<div id='poem_sentence_14_58605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_58605'>平生梦寐处，恍若登华胥。<div id='poem_sentence_15_58605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_58605'>归来拜绿章，足力尚有馀。<div id='poem_sentence_16_58605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_58605'>珍馆十六所，安能遍遨娱。<div id='poem_sentence_17_58605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_58605'>穷探恨不尽，大息仍踟躇<span class='inlineComment2'>（元刘大彬《茅山志》卷二九）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_18_58605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_58605'></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_58605_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
都昌
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ad7b4b6166b945e3953639f0bc491433_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ad7b4b6166b945e3953639f0bc491433");'><span id='ad7b4b6166b945e3953639f0bc491433_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年</a>，58岁</div><div id='ad7b4b6166b945e3953639f0bc491433' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年1月</a>　正月，为江东仓，行部至都昌;应释祖登之邀，为都昌祗园禅院作记。作品：《轮藏记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（尤桐《锡山尤氏丛刊·甲集》）</span><div id='poem_1258659' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258659' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258659?labeling=true' target='_blank'>轮藏记</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙八年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258659")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258659_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258659'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258659'>祇园禅院在唐初曰宝林寺，以旧碑考之，盖预章王陈叔英所建。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258659_comment'></div>贞观中易名长山，本朝治平二年赐今额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258659_comment'></div>曩以甲乙住持，绍兴甲寅，僧晓珂更律焉禅，凡所以安众作佛事者次第葺，独经藏未具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258659_comment'></div>自珂而下，十五代至惟信，信志愿勇决，乃度地于法堂之西庑，募邑檀施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258659_comment'></div>有谭政通者施钱百万为倡，僧振源以五十万继之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258659_comment'></div>于是远近响应，施者云集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258659_comment'></div>以乾道癸巳度材，以淳熙甲午庀工，阅三岁而藏成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258659_comment'></div>遣人持金币募经于福州，外置其上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1258659_comment'></div>未几而信卒，瓦甓之工，丹雘之饰犹未就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1258659_comment'></div>丁酉冬，僧祖登来嗣其席，益募众缘绪成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1258659_comment'></div>其制函受帙，室受函。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1258659_comment'></div>经之帙五千四十有八，而为函已有八十有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1258659_comment'></div>大木中立，众材辐辏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1258659_comment'></div>室则环附如纲目，如弈局。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1258659_comment'></div>阴为机关，激轮运转，其崇二十有五尺，其周八面寻有五寸，上为毗卢遮那，宫殿楼阁充满虚空境界中，为善财参五十三善知识，因地下为八大龙神舒爪运肘之势，其外覆以大殿，广容其藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1258659_comment'></div>琢刻精巧，藻绘严饰，丹垩辉映，过而礼者，动心骇目，以为三昧力所变幻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1258659_comment'></div>计其费至一千万以上，自癸巳迄庚子，阅七寒暑乃成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1258659_comment'></div>非用力之勤，立志之坚，安能建立振起如是其伟哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1258659_comment'></div>余行部至都昌，尝憩于寺，始识登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1258659_comment'></div>登乞余文以记始末，乃为随喜而说偈言：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1258659'>如来得道超人天，妙处不以文字传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1258659_comment'></div>悯诸众生堕迷顽，流浪生死无由还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1258659_comment'></div>方便圆觉开冥昏，如热得濯渴饮泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1258659_comment'></div>尔时大会孤独园，天魔恶叉鬼与仙，长跪合爪祈一言，妙音演秘澎海翻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1258659_comment'></div>欢喜信受敢弗虔，东人震旦知几年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1258659_comment'></div>重翻累译义乃宣，展转传受文益繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1258659_comment'></div>后来卷帙踰五千，纷乱错杂不可删。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1258659_comment'></div>广抄疏义寻真源，蝇触窗纸何由穿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1258659_comment'></div>或欲悟入离声闻，以手提影无控抟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1258659_comment'></div>操戈相攻律与禅，岂知妙本同一关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1258659_comment'></div>皮肤剥落见本源，犹得鱼兔忘蹄筌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1258659_comment'></div>爰有长者众中尊，于末法中度有缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1258659_comment'></div>合成一藏罗宝函，如大海聚金玉渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1258659_comment'></div>取者厌足愿者圆，法轮光转经亦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1258659_comment'></div>一弹指倾遍大千，种种妙义悉现前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1258659_comment'></div>宝林其刹今福田，道人为众愿力坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1258659_comment'></div>欲作大事张空拳，幻成殿阁丹碧鲜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1258659_comment'></div>牙签锦带联巨编，涂金间髹妙庄严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1258659_comment'></div>诸善知识参后先，幢幡宝铎相绕环。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1258659_comment'></div>机发于踵枢贯巅，八龙扶护形蜿蜒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1258659_comment'></div>日月出没天左旋，鬼工神机惊庸凡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1258659_comment'></div>远近来施不吝悭，动以亿万縻金钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1258659_comment'></div>成此胜事顾眄间，此岂智巧能更旃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1258659_comment'></div>佛力广大周无边，我愿众生培善根。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1258659_comment'></div>證此宝藏秘密篇，一超直入三昧门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1258659_comment'></div>成就功德无唐捐，洹河沙劫离垢缠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1258659_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_1258659'>淳熙八年正月，尤袤记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1258659_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年1月28日</a>　正月行部至都昌;二十八日夜，大雪，有诗。作品：《正月二十八日夜大雪》<span class='inlineComment2'>（元·方回《瀛奎律髓》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_58561' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58561' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58561?labeling=true' target='_blank'>正月二十八日夜大雪</a><span class='authorDate'>（辛丑）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_58561")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58561_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58561'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58561'>一冬无雪润田畴，渴井泉源冻不流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58561'>昨夜忽飞三尺雪，今年须兆十分秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58561'>占时父老应先喜，忍冻饥民莫漫愁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58561'>晴色已回春气候，晚风摇绿看来牟<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上同上书卷二一）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58561'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58561_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
南昌（隆兴府）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c32c9eb3b05141e2b5460dc3696149cf_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c32c9eb3b05141e2b5460dc3696149cf");'><span id='c32c9eb3b05141e2b5460dc3696149cf_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年</a>　除江西路转运判官，重建转运司养济院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年7月</a>　在隆兴府任转运判官，七月，进直秘阁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年</a>　在隆兴府任转运判官，与周必大札子，论及辖下十三县第四、第五等残零苗米。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年2月25日</a>　在隆兴府任转运判官，二月二十五日，遣人致祭吕祖谦。作品：《祭直阁大著郎中吕公文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吕祖谦《东莱吕太史文集》附录卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1258669' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258669' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258669?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭直阁大著郎中吕公文</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙九年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258669")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258669_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258669'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258669'>维淳熙九年岁次壬寅二月壬寅朔，二十五日丙寅，朝奉大夫、直秘阁、江南西路转运判官尤袤，谨遣人以清酌之奠，致祭于故宫使直阁大著郎中吕公之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258669_comment'></div>惟公渊源之学，浩养之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258669_comment'></div>纯全之行，刚毅之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258669_comment'></div>高视古人，不论今世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258669_comment'></div>濂溪河南，其道未坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258669_comment'></div>公生百年，独探其秘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258669_comment'></div>障堤末流，折衷六艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258669_comment'></div>斯文是赖，绝学有继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1258669_comment'></div>人言相门，必复其始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1258669_comment'></div>公所抱负，表表愈伟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1258669_comment'></div>谓当亿龄，世济其美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1258669_comment'></div>云胡不淑，而止于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1258669_comment'></div>呜呼天乎，君子何厉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1258669_comment'></div>自我识公，于今三纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1258669_comment'></div>史馆从游，恍若梦寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1258669_comment'></div>去岁池阳，敬遣行李。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1258669_comment'></div>问公起居，得公报字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1258669_comment'></div>遗墨未乾，遽隔生死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1258669_comment'></div>顾瞻门墙，渺邈千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1258669_comment'></div>敛不抚棺，葬不临隧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1258669_comment'></div>一奠寄哀，久乃克致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1258669_comment'></div>追惟平生，有愧明义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1258669_comment'></div>英灵若存，鉴我诚意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1258669_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1258669_comment'></div>伏惟尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1258669_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1258669'><span class='label'>按：</span>《东莱吕太史文集》附录卷二，绩金华丛书本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1258669_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　迁江西漕兼知隆兴府;秋日，与赵蕃会，论及诗学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年9月10日</a>　任江西漕兼知隆兴府，九月初十日，为《吕氏家塾读诗记》作序。作品：《〈吕氏家塾读诗记〉序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·吕祖谦《吕氏家塾读诗记》（《四部丛刊续编》本）卷末。）</span><div id='poem_1258646' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258646' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258646?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吕氏家塾读诗记序</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙九年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258646")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258646_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258646'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258646'>六经遭秦火，多断缺，惟三百篇幸而获全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258646_comment'></div>汉兴，言《诗》者三家，毛氏最著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258646_comment'></div>后世求诗人之意于千百载之下，异论纷纭，莫知折衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258646_comment'></div>东莱吕伯恭病之，因取诸儒之说，择其善者萃为一书，间或断以己意，于是学者始知所归一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258646_comment'></div>今东州士子家宝其书，而编帙既多，传写易误。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258646_comment'></div>建宁所刻，盖又脱遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258646_comment'></div>其友丘漕宗卿惜其传之未广，始锓木于江西漕台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258646_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1258646_comment'></div>伯恭自少年嚅哜道真，涵泳圣涯，至以此得疾且死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1258646_comment'></div>六经皆有论著，未就，独此书粗备，诚不可使其无传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1258646_comment'></div>虽伯恭之学不止于是，然使学者因是书以求先王所以厚人伦、美教化，君子之所以事君事父，则于圣学之门户，岂小补哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1258646_comment'></div>淳熙壬寅重阳后一日，锡山尤袤书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1258646_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　任江西漕兼知隆兴府，王淮荐于朝。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年10月2日</a>　十月初二日，在江西漕台刻成《申鉴》五卷，有题辞。作品：《〈申鉴〉题辞》<span class='inlineComment2'>（汉·荀悦《申鉴》（明正德十三年李濂刻本）附录。）</span><div id='poem_1258647' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258647' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258647?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申鉴题辞</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳熙九年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258647")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258647_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258647'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258647'>荀悦书五卷，观其言，盖有志于经世者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258647_comment'></div>其自著《汉纪》尝载其略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258647_comment'></div>而范晔《东汉书》亦摘其篇首数百言，见之悦传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258647_comment'></div>今《汉纪》会稽郡已版行，而此书则世罕见全本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258647_comment'></div>余家有之，因刻置江西漕台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258647_comment'></div>但简编脱缪，字画差舛者不一，不敢以意增损，疑则阙之，以俟知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258647_comment'></div>淳熙九年冬十月己亥，锡山尤袤。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1258647_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　在江西漕台重刻张方平《玉堂集》二十卷。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　任江西漕兼知隆兴府，与朱熹论字法。作品：《论字法》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·朱熹《晦庵先生朱文公文集》卷八二。原作已佚。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　任江西漕兼知隆兴府，与陆九渊书函往来，论及朱熹救荒之政。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　任江西漕兼知隆兴府，评论杨万里《竹枝歌》等诗，认为接近唐人刘禹锡的风格。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年</a>　任江西漕兼知隆兴府，举荐汪义和通判绍兴府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年</a>　任江西漕兼知隆兴府，请释元聪为庐山云居寺住持。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
新干（新淦）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='33920baa3692427bb9f989602bfd3d98_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("33920baa3692427bb9f989602bfd3d98");'><span id='33920baa3692427bb9f989602bfd3d98_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年</a>，60岁</div><div id='33920baa3692427bb9f989602bfd3d98' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年</a>　游历阁皂山，有诗。作品：《游阁皂山》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·陈思《两宋名贤小集》卷二二三《遂初小稿》尤袤游历、创作的具体时间难以确定，因阁皂山在江西境内，据尤袤江西任官之下限，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_92435' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_92435' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/92435?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游閤皂山<span class='inlineComment2'>（《诗人玉屑》卷一九作刘遂初诗）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1183年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_92435")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_92435_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_92435'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_92435'>春山灵草百花香，谁识仙家日月长。<div id='poem_sentence_0_92435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_92435'>满院莓苔绿阴匝，棋声何处隔宫墙<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_92435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_92435'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_92435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_92435'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_92435_0'>⑴ 以上宋陈思《两宋名贤小集》卷二二三《遂初小稿》</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_92435_comment'></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
鄱阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8ad80b9acb404df18e962d5489e9c84d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8ad80b9acb404df18e962d5489e9c84d");'><span id='8ad80b9acb404df18e962d5489e9c84d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年</a>，60岁</div><div id='8ad80b9acb404df18e962d5489e9c84d' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>屡请祠，进直敷文阁，改江东提刑。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>提刑江东，与曾三复书函往来。作品：《与曾侍郎无玷书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（清·秦瀛《无锡金匮县志》卷四〇。）</span><div id='poem_1258631' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258631' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258631?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与曾侍郎无玷书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1183年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258631")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258631_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258631'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258631'>袤讲闻高义之日久矣，得赵宪景明书，说足下不容口，益起思贤之念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258631_comment'></div>恨相去远，未得承颜接辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258631_comment'></div>乃辱惠诲，不胜感慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258631_comment'></div>窃窥藻丽，益知所缊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1258631_comment'></div>袤承乏于此，得同王事，惧不闻过，凡有可以镌切者勿惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1258631_comment'></div>自此片纸往复，勿用俗礼，乃幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1258631_comment'></div>目昏臂疼，不能尽复来贶，草此一纸为报，殊愧率略也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1258631_comment'></div>袤顿首。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1258631_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
金华（婺州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='9783bdd24e1c4601a17aa57234fb8c17_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9783bdd24e1c4601a17aa57234fb8c17");'><span id='9783bdd24e1c4601a17aa57234fb8c17_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1191')">1190-1191年</a>，67-68岁</div><div id='9783bdd24e1c4601a17aa57234fb8c17' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1190')">1190年7月</a>　起知婺州;七月，同年友人王师愈卒，为其撰诔辞。作品：《中奉大夫直焕章阁王公诔辞》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·王柏《鲁斋集》卷一七《复陈本斋》原作已佚。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1190')">1190年10月</a>　知婺州，十月，朱熹寄赠其于临漳郡斋刻印之“四经”;与吴仁杰论《易》古经。作品：《与吴斗南书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·尤袤《梁溪遗稿》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1258629' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258629' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258629?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与吴斗南书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1190年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258629")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258629_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258629'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258629'>顷得吕东莱所定《古易》一编，朱元晦为之跋，当以板行，乃与左右所刊吕汲公《古经》无毫发异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258629_comment'></div>而东莱不及微仲，尝编此书，岂偶然同邪？</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1258629_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1190')">1190年</a>　知婺州，陆九渊侄陆焕之登门拜见，转达其问候书函。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1190')">1190年</a>　知婺州，复刊尹洙《河南集》，有跋。作品：《〈河南集〉跋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·尹洙《河南集》（《四库全书》本）附录。）</span><div id='poem_1258650' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1258650' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1258650?labeling=true' target='_blank'>河南集跋<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍熙元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1190年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25130, "南宋", "尤袤", "poem_title_1258650")'>尤袤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1258650_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1258650'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1258650'>师鲁集二十卷，承旨姚公手录本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1258650_comment'></div>予往刻师鲁文百篇于会稽行台，今乃得阅其全集，甚慰，因复梓行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1258650_comment'></div>我朝古文之盛，倡自师鲁，一再传而后有欧阳氏、王氏、曾氏，然则师鲁其师资云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1258650_comment'></div>绍熙庚戌，锡山尤袤延之跋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1258650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1258650'><span class='label'>按：</span>《河南集》附录，四库全书本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1258650_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1191&endYear=1191')">1191年3月15日</a>　知婺州，三月十五日，跋李结《西塞渔社图卷》作品：《〈西塞渔社图卷〉跋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·李结《西塞渔社图卷》（美国纽约大都会艺术博物馆藏））</span><br /></div>
-----end
